OVN 22.03 (2022) t√≠ch hŠĽ£p BFD echo native trong pipeline (tr∆įŠĽõc ńĎ√≥ BFD cŠļßn punt ra ovn-controller userspace). OVN 23.06 (2023) th√™m hŠĽó trŠĽ£ ICMP rate-limit ńĎŠĽÉ chŠĽĎng ICMP flood.

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage logic 3 ‚áí OF table 11. ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LR_IN_LOOKUP_NEIGHBOR` (logical 1) + `LR_IN_LEARN_NEIGHBOR` (logical 2), tr∆įŠĽõc `LR_IN_DEFRAG` (logical 4). Scope: per-packet, chŠĽČ packet c√≥ `eth.dst == <LRP_MAC> && ip.dst == <LRP_IP>` mŠĽõi match priority cao tŠļ°i ńĎ√Ęy; packet kh√°c fall through priority 0 next sang stage routing.

**Vai tr√≤.** Vai tr√≤ ch√≠nh: **router self-service** ‚ÄĒ phŠļ£n hŠĽďi tŠļ•t cŠļ£ packet ńĎ√≠ch ńĎŠļŅn router (ICMP, ARP cho LRP IP, BFD echo). Vai tr√≤ phŠĽ•: **error generator** ‚ÄĒ sinh ICMP error (TTL-exceeded tŠĽę stage routing trŠļ£ vŠĽĀ, destination-unreachable cho fragment-needed). PhŠļ°m vi Šļ£nh h∆įŠĽüng: per-packet; c√≥ thŠĽÉ sinh th√™m packet mŠĽõi (reply) qua `clone` action.

**V√¨ sao sinh ra.** Linux router xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ packet self-destination qua netfilter INPUT chain ‚Üí kernel ICMP handler. OVN cŠļßn l√†m t∆į∆°ng ńĎ∆į∆°ng trong pipeline data plane ńĎŠĽÉ: (a) tr√°nh punt mŠĽći ping packet ra userspace (tŠĽĎn k√©m), (b) ńĎŠļ£m bŠļ£o PMTUD nhanh ńĎŠĽÉ tenant TCP kh√īng stuck vŠĽõi MTU sai, (c) BFD echo cŠļßn response trong < 1ms ńĎŠĽÉ health-check kh√īng false-down. Pain point cŇ© (Neutron-OVS + namespace router): mŠĽći self-traffic phŠļ£i qua kernel chain ‚Üí slow. OVN inline trong pipeline ‚Üí fast path datapath.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** CŠĽ• thŠĽÉ: trŠļ£ lŠĽĚi packet ńĎ√≠ch router m√† kh√īng cŠļßn punt ra userspace. C√°ch giŠļ£i: h√†m `build_lrouter_ipv4_ip_input` + `build_lrouter_ipv6_ip_input` (`northd/northd.c`) iterate mŠĽći LRP, sinh flow priority cao match tŠĽęng IP cŠĽßa LRP cho tŠĽęng loŠļ°i request:

- ICMP echo request ‚Üí `clone { eth.src/dst swap; ip.src/dst swap; icmp4.type = 0; next; }` ‚Üí reply ngay
- TTL = 1 ‚Üí `icmp4_error` action sinh ICMP time-exceeded
- Fragment-needed ‚Üí `icmp4_error` vŠĽõi type=3 code=4 + next-hop MTU
- ARP request c√≥ `arp.tpa == <LRP_IP>` ‚Üí trŠļ£ ARP reply vŠĽõi LRP MAC
- BFD echo destination = LRP IP ‚Üí respond trong pipeline

PhŠļ°m vi giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt: chŠĽČ self-traffic; forwarded traffic ńĎi tiŠļŅp sang `LR_IN_DEFRAG` ‚Üí `LR_IN_IP_ROUTING`.

**Importance.** A central pipeline stage. The health check (pinging the gateway) depends on this stage; PMTUD (fragment-needed responses) depends on this stage; the BFD chassis health-check depends on this stage. The engineer must understand that ICMP echo is answered automatically by the pipeline, not by the Linux kernel; that the PMTUD ICMP is generated directly in the pipeline; and that the BFD echo path differs from the BFD control session (the control session is still punted). Without this stage, the class of bug "ping to the gateway shows 100 percent loss but routing is OK" will be debugged in the wrong place.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** Flow ti√™u biŠĽÉu cho LRP `lrp1` IP 10.0.0.1:

```
table=3 (lr_in_ip_input), priority=90,
  match=(ip4.dst == 10.0.0.1 && icmp4.type == 8 && icmp4.code == 0),
  action=(ip4.dst <-> ip4.src;     /* swap */
          ip.ttl = 255;
          icmp4.type = 0;
          eth.dst <-> eth.src;
          inport = "";              /* trigger ovn-controller resubmit */
          flags.loopback = 1;
          outport = <inport_orig>;
          output;)

table=3 (lr_in_ip_input), priority=85,
  match=(ip.ttl == {0, 1} && !ip.later_frag),
  action=(icmp4_error { ... type=11 ... };  /* TTL exceeded */
          drop;)

table=3 (lr_in_ip_input), priority=80,
  match=(reg9[1] == 1 && ip4),         /* fragment-needed flag tŠĽę stage tr∆įŠĽõc */
  action=(icmp4_error { type=3; code=4; "next-hop mtu" = <mtu>; };
          drop;)

table=3 (lr_in_ip_input), priority=90,
  match=(arp.op == 1 && arp.tpa == 10.0.0.1),
  action=(eth.dst = eth.src;
          eth.src = RR:RR:RR:RR:RR:01;
          arp.op = 2;
          arp.tha = arp.sha;
          arp.sha = RR:RR:RR:RR:RR:01;
          arp.tpa = arp.spa;
          arp.spa = 10.0.0.1;
          outport = inport;
          flags.loopback = 1;
          output;)

table=3 (lr_in_ip_input), priority=0,
  match=(1),
  action=(next;)
```

Action `clone {}` cho ph√©p sinh packet mŠĽõi (reply) m√† kh√īng drop original (mŠļ∑c d√Ļ trong ICMP echo case, packet original ch√≠nh l√† packet ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c swap th√†nh reply). Action `icmp4_error` consult `controller/pinctrl.c` ńĎŠĽÉ build ICMP error mŠĽõi chŠĽ©a header packet gŠĽĎc 28 byte. Invariant: nŠļŅu packet match priority cao tŠļ°i ńĎ√Ęy, n√≥ **kh√īng** ńĎi tiŠļŅp sang routing; nŠļŅu match priority 0 (`next;`), ńĎi tiŠļŅp pipeline.

**C√°ch kŠĽĻ s∆į vŠļ≠n h√†nh th√†nh thŠļ°o.** (1) **ńźŠĽćc**: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr1 | grep lr_in_ip_input` thŠļ•y nh√°nh ICMP / TTL / fragment / ARP. (2) **SŠĽ≠a**: bŠļ≠t/tŠļĮt PMTUD qua `Logical_Router.options:pmtud_enabled`. (3) **Quan s√°t**: `ovn-trace lr1 'inport=="lrp1" && ip4.dst==10.0.0.1 && icmp4.type==8'` xem stage 3 c√≥ swap header. (4) **Debug**: nŠļŅu ping gateway fail, ńĎŠļŅm `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=11 | grep n_packets` priority 90 ICMP ‚ÄĒ nŠļŅu n_packets kh√īng tńÉng khi ping ‚Üí packet kh√īng ńĎŠļŅn ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c table 11 (vŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ stage tr∆įŠĽõc).

**Ph√Ęn loŠļ°i.** LoŠļ°i stage: **router self-handler** (subtype "L3 endpoint service"). Kh√°c `LS_IN_DHCP_OPTIONS` (DHCP cho LS), `LR_IN_DNAT` (NAT, ph√≠a sau). Stateful nhŠļĻ (kh√īng touch conntrack) ‚ÄĒ chŠĽČ touch packet, sinh reply.

**Quy tr√¨nh sŠĽ≠ dŠĽ•ng.**
1. `ovn-nbctl lr-add lr1`
2. `ovn-nbctl lrp-add lr1 lrp1 RR:01 10.0.0.1/24`
3. (optional) `ovn-nbctl set Logical_Router lr1 options:pmtud_enabled=true`
4. (optional BFD) `ovn-nbctl create BFD logical_port=lrp1 dst_ip=10.0.0.250 status=admin_up`
5. Verify: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr1 | grep lr_in_ip_input` thŠļ•y nh√°nh ICMP echo
6. Test: tŠĽę VM 10.0.0.5 ‚Üí `ping 10.0.0.1` ‚Üí xem reply trŠĽü vŠĽĀ (count = count_send)
7. Test PMTUD: gŠĽ≠i packet > MTU vŠĽõi DF set ‚Üí verify ICMP fragment-needed reply

**Khi xŠļ£y ra sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ.** Symptom: (a) "Ping gateway loss 100%" ‚Üí step 1: ovn-trace verify packet ńĎŠļŅn table 11, step 2: nŠļŅu ńĎŠļŅn nh∆įng kh√īng match priority 90, kiŠĽÉm tra ip4.dst trong packet so vŠĽõi LRP_IP, step 3: xem Logical_Router.options. (b) "PMTUD broken (TCP stuck vŠĽõi MTU sai)" ‚Üí check `pmtud_enabled` option + flow priority 80 fragment-needed. (c) "BFD session flapping" ‚Üí kiŠĽÉm tra BFD echo c√≥ ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c respond kh√īng (ńĎŠļŅm flow BFD priority 90).

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** Tightly coupled: `Logical_Router_Port.networks` (LRP IP source), `Logical_Router.options:pmtud_enabled`, `BFD` table NBDB, `controller/pinctrl.c` (xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ icmp4_error generate), `LR_IN_LOOKUP_NEIGHBOR` (stage liŠĽĀn tr∆įŠĽõc, populate MAC_Binding cache). Loose: VRRP/HSRP (alternative router redundancy ngo√†i OVN), routing protocol nh∆į OSPF/RIP (sentence-level mention only ‚ÄĒ banned scope per North Star).

**Kh√°c biŠĽát giŠĽĮa c√°c phi√™n bŠļ£n.**
- OVN 2.5 (2015): chŠĽČ ICMP echo + ARP responder
- OVN 20.06 (2020): th√™m fragment-needed (PMTUD) qua `icmp4_error` action
- OVN 21.03 (2021): consolidate ARP responder v√†o stage n√†y (tr∆įŠĽõc ńĎ√≥ ŠĽü stage ri√™ng)
- OVN 22.03 (2022): BFD echo native, kh√īng cŠļßn punt
- OVN 23.06 (2023): ICMP rate-limit option chŠĽĎng flood
- OVN 24.03 (2024): th√™m hŠĽó trŠĽ£ ICMPv6 redirect cho IPv6

**C√°ch quan s√°t + x√°c minh.**

```
$ ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr1 | grep "lr_in_ip_input"
  table=3 (lr_in_ip_input), priority=90,
    match=(ip4.dst == 10.0.0.1 && icmp4.type == 8 && icmp4.code == 0),
    action=(ip4.dst <-> ip4.src; ip.ttl = 255; icmp4.type = 0;
            eth.dst <-> eth.src; outport = inport;
            flags.loopback = 1; output;)

$ ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=11 | grep "metadata=0x7"
  cookie=0x..., table=11, n_packets=42, priority=90,
    metadata=0x7,icmp,nw_dst=10.0.0.1,icmp_type=8,icmp_code=0,
    actions=...

$ ovn-trace lr1 'inport=="lrp1" && eth.src==aa:aa && eth.dst==rr:01 && ip4 && ip4.src==10.0.0.5 && ip4.dst==10.0.0.1 && icmp4.type==8'
  ‚Üí ingress(dp="lr1", inport="lrp1")
    3. lr_in_ip_input (priority=90, ICMP echo)
       eth.dst <-> eth.src; ip4.dst <-> ip4.src; icmp4.type = 0;
       output;
```

**Source code.** Tham chiŠļŅu OVN branch-22.03:
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lrouter_ipv4_ip_input()`: h√†m ch√≠nh cho IPv4
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lrouter_ipv6_ip_input()`: h√†m ch√≠nh cho IPv6
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lrouter_force_snat_for_lb()`: t∆į∆°ng t√°c vŠĽõi LB DNAT (nŠļŅu LB chŠĽČ tŠĽõi LRP IP)
- `lib/lflow.h` `S_ROUTER_IN_IP_INPUT = 3`: stage id
- `controller/pinctrl.c` `pinctrl_handle_icmp4_error()`: generator ICMP error

**Tr∆įŠĽĚng hŠĽ£p sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ.** Q4/2024 production: NOC b√°o "ping gateway loss intermittent ~30% tŠĽę tenant subnet sau scale-up cluster". Investigation: `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=11 | grep n_packets` priority 90 ICMP echo nhŠļ£y nh∆įng kh√īng bŠļĪng sŠĽĎ ping gŠĽ≠i. ThŠĽ≠ `ovn-trace`: kŠļŅt quŠļ£ OK. ChŠļ°y `tcpdump` tr√™n LRP tap interface: thŠļ•y ICMP echo ńĎŠļŅn nh∆įng ńĎ√īi khi kh√īng c√≥ reply ra. Root cause: ICMP rate-limit (option mŠĽõi enable nhŠļßm vŠĽõi threshold 100/s m√† workload tenant gŠĽ≠i 200/s ping monitoring) ‚Üí packet v∆įŠĽ£t threshold drop tŠļ°i stage n√†y. Fix: tńÉng `icmp_rate_limit` l√™n 1000/s hoŠļ∑c disable cho tenant ńĎŠļ∑c biŠĽát. Cross-link PhŠļßn 13.18 ¬ßicmp4_error.

**B√†i tŠļ≠p synthetic.**

```bash
sudo ovn-nbctl lr-add lr-lab
sudo ovn-nbctl lrp-add lr-lab lrp-lab RR:11:11:11:11:11 10.0.0.1/24
sudo ovn-nbctl ls-add ls-lab
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-lab ls-lab-to-lr
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-set-type ls-lab-to-lr router
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-set-options ls-lab-to-lr router-port=lrp-lab
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-set-addresses ls-lab-to-lr router
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-lab vm1
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-set-addresses vm1 "AA:01 10.0.0.5"
# Lab task 1: ping 10.0.0.1 tŠĽę vm1 ‚Üí verify reply (stage 3 ICMP echo)
# Lab task 2: gŠĽ≠i packet vŠĽõi TTL=1 tŠĽõi mŠĽôt IP xa ‚Üí verify ICMP TTL-exceeded reply (stage 3 priority 85)
# Lab task 3: gŠĽ≠i UDP packet > MTU vŠĽõi DF set tŠĽõi destination ngo√†i ‚Üí verify ICMP fragment-needed reply
# Lab task 4: ARP who-has 10.0.0.1 ‚Üí verify ARP reply vŠĽõi MAC RR:11
```

**LŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p + t√≠n hiŠĽáu chŠļ©n ńĎo√°n.**
- Mode A "ping gateway loss": stage 3 ICMP priority 90 kh√īng match ‚Üí kiŠĽÉm tra `ip4.dst == LRP_IP` ch√≠nh x√°c
- Mode B "PMTUD broken": pmtud_enabled false ‚Üí set true; hoŠļ∑c fragment-needed packet bŠĽč filter giŠĽĮa ńĎ∆įŠĽĚng (network thŠĽĪc)
- Mode C "BFD echo kh√īng respond": OVN < 22.03 kh√īng c√≥ inline BFD ‚Üí upgrade hoŠļ∑c fall back ovn-controller userspace
- Mode D "ICMP rate-limit drop legit traffic": adjust `icmp_rate_limit` option (OVN 23.06+)
- Mode E "ARP responder kh√īng trŠļ£ lŠĽĚi": LRP MAC trong NBDB sai hoŠļ∑c kh√īng khŠĽõp vŠĽõi eth.src expected ‚Üí reconcile

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Linux router netfilter INPUT chain analog: c√Ļng xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ packet ńĎ√≠ch router (ICMP, TCP self-port, ARP). Kh√°c: Linux d√Ļng kernel chain qua slow path; OVN inline trong datapath fast path. Cisco IOS "punt to RP" model t∆į∆°ng tŠĽĪ nh∆įng RP CPU bottleneck; OVN distribute tr√™n mŠĽći hypervisor. NSX-T DR self-traffic handler c√Ļng pattern. Routing protocol nh∆į OSPF/BGP (mention only, kh√īng deep-dive theo North Star ban) th∆įŠĽĚng vŠļęn punt ra userspace daemon FRR/Quagga, kh√īng inline OVN pipeline.

---

## ¬ß13.19.9 LR_IN_DNAT ‚ÄĒ Destination NAT tr√™n ingress LR (floating IP, port forwarding)

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LR_IN_DNAT` l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 6** (OF table 14) ‚ÄĒ n∆°i thŠĽĪc hiŠĽán **Destination NAT** tr√™n Logical_Router theo `NAT.type == "dnat"` hoŠļ∑c `NAT.type == "dnat_and_snat"` (floating IP). Match `ip.dst == <external_ip>` ‚Üí `ct(commit, nat(dst=<logical_ip>))` ‚Üí packet sau stage n√†y c√≥ dst ńĎ√£ rewrite vŠĽĀ internal IP, conntrack entry committed ńĎŠĽÉ reply path biŠļŅt undo. LoŠļ°i: **pipeline stage cornerstone**, sub-loŠļ°i "north-south DNAT + floating IP".

**LŠĽčch sŠĽ≠ + bŠĽĎi cŠļ£nh.** OVN 2.4 (2015) introduce NAT centralized tr√™n gateway chassis (DNAT + SNAT chŠĽČ chŠļ°y ŠĽü chassis ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c redirect). OVN 21.06 (2021) introduce **distributed NAT** (`dnat_and_snat` chŠļ°y tr√™n mŠĽći hypervisor c√≥ VM nŠļĪm sau floating IP, loŠļ°i bŠĽŹ choke point gateway chassis). OVN 22.03 (2022) th√™m option `force_snat_for_dnat` (cho ph√©p kŠļŅt hŠĽ£p DNAT + SNAT ńĎŠĽÉ giŠļ£i pet hairpin). OVN 23.06 (2023) t√≠ch hŠĽ£p `Load_Balancer` + NAT: nŠļŅu LB VIP tr√Ļng NAT external_ip, LB DNAT ∆įu ti√™n h∆°n NAT DNAT (h√†m `build_lrouter_nat_flows_for_lb`). OVN 24.03 (2024) th√™m hŠĽó trŠĽ£ NAT cho IPv6.

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage logic 6 ‚áí OF table 14. ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LR_IN_DEFRAG` (logical 4) + `LR_IN_UNSNAT` (logical 5), tr∆įŠĽõc `LR_IN_ECMP_STATEFUL` (logical 7). Scope: per-packet, per-LR datapath. Quan trŠĽćng: chŠĽČ packet north-bound (tŠĽę external v√†o internal) match priority cao tŠļ°i ńĎ√Ęy; packet east-west fall through priority 0 next.

**Vai tr√≤.** Vai tr√≤ ch√≠nh: **DNAT enforcement** ‚ÄĒ rewrite `ip.dst` tŠĽę external IP (floating IP) sang internal IP cŠĽßa VM. Vai tr√≤ phŠĽ•: **conntrack commit** ‚ÄĒ tŠļ°o entry trong `nf_conntrack` zone cŠĽßa LR ńĎŠĽÉ reply path (`LR_OUT_UNDNAT` ŠĽü stage 1 egress) tŠĽĪ ńĎŠĽông undo DNAT. PhŠļ°m vi Šļ£nh h∆įŠĽüng: lifetime cŠĽßa connection (entry tŠĽďn tŠļ°i ńĎŠļŅn timeout conntrack).

**V√¨ sao sinh ra.** Cloud workload cŠļßn expose VM l√™n Internet vŠĽõi public IP ri√™ng (floating IP). Tr∆įŠĽõc OVN, OpenStack Neutron-OVS d√Ļng iptables DNAT trong network node namespace ‚Üí SPoF + slow. OVN abstract th√†nh stage trong pipeline, ńĎi k√®m distributed DNAT (`dnat_and_snat`) cho ph√©p mŠĽói hypervisor tŠĽĪ xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ NAT cho VM cŠĽßa m√¨nh ‚Üí loŠļ°i choke point. Ngo√†i ra, distributed NAT giŠļ£m latency 1 hop (kh√īng qua gateway chassis).

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** CŠĽ• thŠĽÉ: rewrite dst IP + commit conntrack atomic. C√°ch giŠļ£i: h√†m `build_lrouter_in_dnat_flow` (`northd/northd.c` d√≤ng ~13067) iterate `NAT` rows cŠĽßa LR, sinh flow priority cao cho mŠĽói row:

- Cho `NAT.type == "dnat"`: match `ip.dst == external_ip`, action `ct_dnat(<logical_ip>)`. Centralized ‚ÄĒ thŠĽĪc thi tŠļ°i gateway chassis sau khi packet ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c redirect.
- Cho `NAT.type == "dnat_and_snat"` (floating IP): match `ip.dst == external_ip`, action `ct_dnat(<logical_ip>)`. Distributed ‚ÄĒ nŠļŅu `Logical_Router.options:always_learn_from_arp_request=true`, mŠĽći hypervisor ńĎŠĽĀu biŠļŅt MAC mapping n√™n c√≥ thŠĽÉ xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ local.

PhŠļ°m vi giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt: chŠĽČ DNAT (rewrite dst); SNAT l√†m ŠĽü stage `LR_OUT_SNAT` (egress); UNDNAT/UNSNAT cho reply path ŠĽü stage egress 1.

**Importance.** A central pipeline stage for cloud north-south workloads. Floating IP, port forwarding, and public service exposure all traverse this stage. The engineer must distinguish centralized DNAT (`dnat`) from distributed DNAT (`dnat_and_snat`), understand the per-LR conntrack zone (which keeps NAT entries from colliding across LRs), and understand the interaction with Load_Balancer.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** Flow ti√™u biŠĽÉu cho NAT row external 1.2.3.4 ‚Üí logical 10.0.0.5:

```
table=6 (lr_in_dnat), priority=100,
  match=(ip4 && ip4.dst == 1.2.3.4 && inport == "lrp-public" && is_chassis_resident("cr-lrp-public")),
  action=(ct_dnat(10.0.0.5);)

table=6 (lr_in_dnat), priority=50,
  match=(ip4 && ip4.dst == 1.2.3.4 && ct.est && ct_label.natted == 1),
  action=(next;)  /* established connection bypass re-DNAT */

table=6 (lr_in_dnat), priority=0,
  match=(1),
  action=(next;)
```

Action `ct_dnat(<ip>)` l√ļc compile xuŠĽĎng OVS th√†nh `ct(commit, table=N, zone=<lr_zone>, nat(dst=<ip>))`. Conntrack commit entry vŠĽõi mapping `1.2.3.4 ‚ÜĒ 10.0.0.5`, ńĎŠĽÉ reply (10.0.0.5 ‚Üí external client) qua stage `LR_OUT_UNDNAT` tŠĽĪ ńĎŠĽông rewrite src vŠĽĀ 1.2.3.4. Predicate `is_chassis_resident("cr-lrp-public")` √©p flow chŠĽČ thŠĽĪc thi tŠļ°i gateway chassis sŠĽü hŠĽĮu LRP public (cho centralized `dnat`) ‚ÄĒ distributed `dnat_and_snat` kh√īng c√≥ predicate n√†y. Invariant: sau stage, packet `dst` ńĎ√£ ńĎŠĽēi sang logical IP; conntrack entry ńĎŠļ£m bŠļ£o reply UNDNAT ńĎ√ļng.

**C√°ch kŠĽĻ s∆į vŠļ≠n h√†nh th√†nh thŠļ°o.** (1) **ńźŠĽćc**: `ovn-nbctl lr-nat-list lr1` xem c√°c NAT row + type + external/logical IP. (2) **SŠĽ≠a**: `ovn-nbctl lr-nat-add lr1 dnat_and_snat 1.2.3.4 10.0.0.5` (floating IP); `ovn-nbctl lr-nat-del lr1 dnat_and_snat 1.2.3.4` ńĎŠĽÉ gŠĽ°. (3) **Quan s√°t**: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<lr_zone> | grep 1.2.3.4` xem entry. (4) **Debug**: `ovn-trace lr1 'inport=="lrp-public" && ip4.dst==1.2.3.4 && ...'` thŠļ•y stage 6 chŠĽćn ct_dnat.

**Ph√Ęn loŠļ°i.** LoŠļ°i stage: **N-S DNAT enforcer** (subtype "stateful destination NAT"). Kh√°c `LS_IN_LB` (LB DNAT tr√™n LS, c√≥ hash_fields), `LR_IN_UNSNAT` (reverse SNAT cho reply, ngay tr∆įŠĽõc stage n√†y), `LR_OUT_SNAT` (forward SNAT, ŠĽü egress).

**Quy tr√¨nh sŠĽ≠ dŠĽ•ng.** Khi expose VM vŠĽõi floating IP:
1. GŠļĮn LRP public: `ovn-nbctl lrp-add lr1 lrp-public RR:99 1.2.3.1/24`
2. Set gateway chassis: `ovn-nbctl lrp-set-gateway-chassis lrp-public chassis-1 100`
3. TŠļ°o NAT row: `ovn-nbctl lr-nat-add lr1 dnat_and_snat 1.2.3.4 10.0.0.5`
4. Verify: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr1 | grep lr_in_dnat` thŠļ•y flow priority 100 cho 1.2.3.4
5. Test: tŠĽę external client `ping 1.2.3.4` ‚Üí packet ńĎŠļŅn VM 10.0.0.5 ‚Üí reply tŠĽĪ ńĎŠĽông UNDNAT
6. Verify conntrack: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack | grep 1.2.3.4` thŠļ•y entry mapping

**Khi xŠļ£y ra sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ.** Symptom: (a) "Floating IP unreachable tŠĽę Internet" ‚Üí step 1: ovn-trace verify stage 6 match priority 100, step 2: nŠļŅu match nh∆įng packet kh√īng ńĎŠļŅn VM, kiŠĽÉm tra conntrack zone c√≥ conflict. (b) "FIP ńĎ√īi khi work, ńĎ√īi khi kh√īng" ‚Üí kiŠĽÉm tra gateway chassis HA ‚ÄĒ nŠļŅu chassis fail, distributed NAT kh√īng c√≥ ARP responder ‚Üí packet rŠĽõt. (c) "FIP work nh∆įng VM kh√īng reply ng∆įŠĽ£c" ‚Üí kiŠĽÉm tra `LR_OUT_UNDNAT` stage egress. (d) "Conntrack table full" ‚Üí `nf_conntrack_count / max > 95%` ‚Üí tńÉng max hoŠļ∑c giŠļ£m timeout. Cross-link: PhŠļßn 13.3 ¬ßNAT compile, PhŠļßn 9.24 ¬ßct_state, PhŠļßn 13.18 ¬ßREGBIT_NAT_REDIRECT.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** Tightly coupled: NBDB `NAT` table (nguŠĽďn dŠĽĮ liŠĽáu), `LR_IN_DEFRAG` (defrag tr∆įŠĽõc NAT, nŠļŅu kh√īng sŠļĹ NAT lŠĽách fragment), `LR_IN_UNSNAT` (reverse SNAT, stage liŠĽĀn tr∆įŠĽõc), `LR_OUT_UNDNAT` + `LR_OUT_SNAT` (egress reverse path), `Load_Balancer` (nŠļŅu VIP tr√Ļng external_ip, LB ∆įu ti√™n), `is_chassis_resident` predicate (x√°c ńĎŠĽčnh gateway chassis), conntrack zone per-LR. Loose: BGP advertisement floating IP (banned scope per North Star ‚ÄĒ chŠĽČ mention cŠļ•p ńĎŠĽô sentence).

**Kh√°c biŠĽát giŠĽĮa c√°c phi√™n bŠļ£n.**
- OVN 2.4 (2015): chŠĽČ `dnat` centralized; phŠļ£i qua gateway chassis
- OVN 21.06 (2021): distributed `dnat_and_snat` ‚ÄĒ chŠļ°y tr√™n mŠĽći hypervisor c√≥ VM target
- OVN 22.03 (2022): option `force_snat_for_dnat` cho hairpin tricky
- OVN 23.06 (2023): LB + NAT integration via `build_lrouter_nat_flows_for_lb`
- OVN 24.03 (2024): NAT cho IPv6; `allowed_ext_ips` option giŠĽõi hŠļ°n external IP nguŠĽďn

**C√°ch quan s√°t + x√°c minh.**

```
$ ovn-nbctl lr-nat-list lr1
  TYPE             EXTERNAL_IP    LOGICAL_IP   EXTERNAL_MAC   LOGICAL_PORT
  dnat_and_snat    1.2.3.4        10.0.0.5     RR:CC:DD       lsp-vm1

$ ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr1 | grep "lr_in_dnat"
  table=6 (lr_in_dnat), priority=100,
    match=(ip4 && ip4.dst == 1.2.3.4 && inport == "lrp-public"
           && is_chassis_resident("cr-lrp-public")),
    action=(ct_dnat(10.0.0.5);)

$ ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=7 | grep 1.2.3.4
  tcp,orig=(src=8.8.8.8,dst=1.2.3.4,sport=4001,dport=80),
       reply=(src=10.0.0.5,dst=8.8.8.8,sport=80,dport=4001),
       protoinfo=(state=ESTABLISHED), zone=7

$ ovn-trace lr1 'inport=="lrp-public" && eth.dst==RR:99 && ip4 && ip4.src==8.8.8.8 && ip4.dst==1.2.3.4 && tcp && tcp.dst==80'
  ‚Üí ingress(dp="lr1", inport="lrp-public")
    6. lr_in_dnat (priority=100)
       ct_dnat(10.0.0.5);
```

**Source code.** Tham chiŠļŅu OVN branch-22.03:
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lrouter_in_dnat_flow()` (d√≤ng ~13067): h√†m ch√≠nh build stage n√†y
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lrouter_in_unsnat_flow()` (d√≤ng ~12987): sibling stage UNSNAT logical 5
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lrouter_nat_defrag_and_lb()` (d√≤ng ~13581): defrag + LB integration
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lrouter_nat_flows_for_lb()` (d√≤ng ~10005): LB ∆įu ti√™n NAT khi VIP tr√Ļng
- `lib/lflow.h` `S_ROUTER_IN_DNAT = 6`: stage id
- `controller/lflow.c` `consider_logical_flow()`: dŠĽčch ct_dnat ‚Üí OVS ct(nat()) action

**Tr∆įŠĽĚng hŠĽ£p sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ.** Q3/2024 production: customer b√°o "floating IP 1.2.3.4 (ńĎńÉng k√Ĺ map v√†o VM 10.0.0.5) reachable tŠĽę Internet nh∆įng intermittent ‚ÄĒ ńĎ√īi l√ļc TCP handshake xong rŠĽďi ngŠļĮt, ńĎ√īi l√ļc connect timeout". Investigation: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=7 | grep 1.2.3.4` thŠļ•y entry tŠĽďn tŠļ°i. tcpdump tr√™n LRP public thŠļ•y SYN ńĎŠļŅn, SYN-ACK ra, sau ńĎ√≥ nhiŠĽĀu ACK retransmit tŠĽę client. Tr√™n VM 10.0.0.5: tcpdump kh√īng thŠļ•y ACK cŠĽßa client. Root cause: conntrack zone cŠĽßa LR + zone cŠĽßa LS conflict (cŠļ£ hai zone d√Ļng c√Ļng sŠĽĎ 7 do bug NBDB schema ch∆įa unique-zone cho mŠĽói datapath khi datapath_count > 100). Reply path SNAT ńĎi qua zone LS rewrite sai ‚Üí packet vŠĽĀ client vŠĽõi sai source. Fix: upgrade l√™n OVN 22.03.5 (commit `7fe21f3a` fixed zone collision) + `ovn-nbctl --wait=hv sync`.

**B√†i tŠļ≠p synthetic.**

```bash
sudo ovn-nbctl lr-add lr-lab
sudo ovn-nbctl lrp-add lr-lab lrp-internal RR:11 10.0.0.1/24
sudo ovn-nbctl lrp-add lr-lab lrp-public RR:99 1.2.3.1/24
sudo ovn-nbctl lrp-set-gateway-chassis lrp-public chassis-1 100
sudo ovn-nbctl ls-add ls-internal
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-internal vm1
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-set-addresses vm1 "AA:01 10.0.0.5"
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-internal ls-to-lr
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-set-type ls-to-lr router
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-set-options ls-to-lr router-port=lrp-internal
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-set-addresses ls-to-lr router
# Lab task 1: lr-nat-add lr-lab dnat_and_snat 1.2.3.4 10.0.0.5 ‚Üí verify stage 6 priority 100
# Lab task 2: tŠĽę external "client" gŠĽ≠i TCP tŠĽõi 1.2.3.4:80 ‚Üí verify packet ńĎŠļŅn vm1 vŠĽõi dst=10.0.0.5
# Lab task 3: dump-conntrack zone cŠĽßa lr-lab ‚Üí verify entry mapping 1.2.3.4 ‚ÜĒ 10.0.0.5
# Lab task 4: lr-nat-del 1.2.3.4 ‚Üí verify connection mŠĽõi drop, connection cŇ© vŠļęn sŠĽĎng (ct.est match priority 50 next)
```

**LŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p + t√≠n hiŠĽáu chŠļ©n ńĎo√°n.**
- Mode A "FIP unreachable ho√†n to√†n": stage 6 kh√īng match priority 100 ‚Üí kiŠĽÉm tra is_chassis_resident predicate + gateway_chassis assignment
- Mode B "Reply path broken": conntrack zone conflict hoŠļ∑c UNDNAT stage egress fail ‚Üí upgrade OVN
- Mode C "Conntrack table full": tńÉng `nf_conntrack_max`; giŠļ£m `tcp_timeout_close_wait`
- Mode D "DNAT bŠĽč LB DNAT override": VIP LB tr√Ļng external_ip NAT ‚Üí review LB+NAT priority (LB win in OVN 23.06+)
- Mode E "Distributed NAT broken cho 1 hypervisor": chassis ch∆įa join Chassis_Private hoŠļ∑c encap ch∆įa ńĎ√ļng ‚Üí check ovn-controller log

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Linux iptables DNAT in PREROUTING analog: c√Ļng pattern match dst ‚Üí rewrite + conntrack track. Kh√°c: iptables centralized tr√™n 1 host, OVN distribute tr√™n mŠĽći hypervisor cho `dnat_and_snat`. Cisco IOS static NAT hoŠļ∑c NAT-PT t∆į∆°ng tŠĽĪ √Ĺ t∆įŠĽüng nh∆įng centralized router. AWS EIP (Elastic IP) t∆į∆°ng ńĎ∆į∆°ng semantic floating IP, managed service. NSX-T DR DNAT distributed gŠļßn giŠĽĎng OVN (c√Ļng motivation loŠļ°i bŠĽŹ choke point).

---

## ¬ß13.19.10 LR_IN_GW_REDIRECT ‚ÄĒ chuyŠĽÉn h∆įŠĽõng N-S traffic vŠĽĀ gateway chassis

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LR_IN_GW_REDIRECT` l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 18** (OF table 26) ‚ÄĒ n∆°i quyŠļŅt ńĎŠĽčnh chuyŠĽÉn h∆įŠĽõng packet **north-south** vŠĽĀ **gateway chassis** (chassis ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c chŠĽČ ńĎŠĽčnh trong `Logical_Router_Port.gateway_chassis` hoŠļ∑c `HA_Chassis_Group`). Match `outport` ńĎang trŠĽŹ tŠĽõi mŠĽôt LRP c√≥ `gateway_chassis` config ‚Üí ńĎŠĽēi outport th√†nh `chassisredirect` Port_Binding (`cr-<LRP>`) ‚Üí packet ńĎi qua tunnel Geneve tŠĽõi gateway chassis, ŠĽü ńĎ√≥ pipeline LR tiŠļŅp tŠĽ•c c√°c stage c√≤n lŠļ°i (NAT egress, ARP resolve cho external network). LoŠļ°i: **pipeline stage cornerstone**, sub-loŠļ°i "distributed gateway redirect".

**LŠĽčch sŠĽ≠ + bŠĽĎi cŠļ£nh.** OVN 2.10 (2018) introduce concept "gateway router" ‚ÄĒ to√†n bŠĽô LR ńĎŠļ∑t tr√™n 1 chassis (centralized). OVN 21.06 (2021) introduce **distributed gateway** vŠĽõi chassisredirect port (`cr-<LRP>`): pipeline LR ph√Ęn t√°n tr√™n mŠĽći hypervisor cho phŠļßn east-west, chŠĽČ nhŠĽĮng stage cŠļßn external (NAT, ARP cho physical network) mŠĽõi redirect vŠĽĀ 1 chassis ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c elect. OVN 22.03 (2022) integrate `HA_Chassis_Group` cho HA failover cŠĽßa gateway chassis (BFD-based). OVN 23.06 (2023) th√™m `redirect-type=bridged` (alternative redirect qua Logical_Switch thay v√¨ Geneve tunnel). OVN 24.03 (2024) tŠĽĎi ∆įu redirect cho LB DNAT (skip redirect nŠļŅu LB chŠĽČ tŠĽõi VM c√Ļng hypervisor).

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage logic 18 ‚áí OF table 26. ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LR_IN_ARP_RESOLVE` (logical 16) + `LR_IN_CHK_PKT_LEN` (logical 17), tr∆įŠĽõc `LR_IN_LARGER_PKTS` (logical 19). Scope: per-packet. ńź√Ęy l√† **ńĎiŠĽÉm chuyŠĽÉn trŠĽćng t√Ęm** giŠĽĮa pipeline distributed (mŠĽći hypervisor) v√† pipeline centralized (chŠĽČ gateway chassis); sau stage n√†y, nŠļŅu redirect, packet chui qua tunnel Geneve ńĎŠĽÉ stage egress chŠļ°y ŠĽü chassis kh√°c.

**Vai tr√≤.** Vai tr√≤ ch√≠nh: **gateway dispatcher** ‚ÄĒ quyŠļŅt ńĎŠĽčnh stage egress LR chŠļ°y local hay tŠļ°i gateway chassis. Vai tr√≤ phŠĽ•: **HA selector** ‚ÄĒ nŠļŅu gateway_chassis c√≥ HA group, chŠĽćn chassis ńĎang up qua BFD. PhŠļ°m vi: 1 packet, Šļ£nh h∆įŠĽüng outport register reg15.

**V√¨ sao sinh ra.** Centralized gateway router (OVN < 21.06) tŠļ°o SPoF + bottleneck CPU (tŠļ•t cŠļ£ N-S traffic qua 1 chassis). Distributed gateway t√°ch th√†nh phŠļßn: stage east-west chŠļ°y local mŠĽói hypervisor (LR_IN_IP_INPUT, IP_ROUTING, ARP cho LRP nŠĽôi bŠĽô); stage cŠļßn external (NAT external_ip, ARP cho IP physical, BFD physical link) cŠļßn single hypervisor ńĎŠĽÉ tr√°nh duplicate ARP / NAT entry race. Stage n√†y l√† "switch" giŠĽĮa 2 pipeline parts.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** CŠĽ• thŠĽÉ: chuyŠĽÉn packet ńĎŠļŅn gateway chassis nŠļŅu outport l√† LRP c√≥ `gateway_chassis` config. C√°ch giŠļ£i: h√†m `build_gateway_redirect_flows_for_lrouter` (`northd/northd.c`) iterate mŠĽći LRP c√≥ `gateway_chassis` non-empty, sinh flow priority 100 match `outport == <LRP> && !is_chassis_resident("cr-<LRP>")` action `outport = "cr-<LRP>"; next;`. `cr-<LRP>` l√† chassisredirect Port_Binding ‚ÄĒ virtual port chŠĽČ tŠĽďn tŠļ°i tr√™n 1 chassis (ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c elect qua BFD HA). Khi outport set tŠĽõi `cr-<LRP>`, OVN encap packet trong Geneve v√† gŠĽ≠i tŠĽõi chassis ńĎ√≥. PhŠļ°m vi: chŠĽČ N-S; east-west kh√īng c√≥ gateway_chassis n√™n priority 0 next, ńĎi tiŠļŅp local.

**Importance.** A central pipeline stage for the distributed gateway architecture, which is the foundation of OVN's scalability. Every production OVN cloud cluster uses this pattern (since OVN 21.06). The engineer must understand that the `chassisredirect` Port_Binding type differs from a regular LSP (see ¬ß13.5b), that the `is_chassis_resident()` predicate means "the chassis currently owns the cr port", and how HA_Chassis_Group failover works via BFD (see ¬ß13.6). Without this stage, the class of bug "VM loses Internet access after a gateway chassis failure" will be debugged in the wrong place.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** Flow ti√™u biŠĽÉu cho LRP `lrp-public` c√≥ gateway_chassis = `chassis-1` (priority 100), `chassis-2` (priority 50):

```
table=18 (lr_in_gw_redirect), priority=100,
  match=(outport == "lrp-public" && !is_chassis_resident("cr-lrp-public")),
  action=(outport = "cr-lrp-public";
          next;)

table=18 (lr_in_gw_redirect), priority=50,
  match=(outport == "lrp-public" && is_chassis_resident("cr-lrp-public")),
  action=(next;)  /* local chassis sŠĽü hŠĽĮu cr port, kh√īng redirect */

table=18 (lr_in_gw_redirect), priority=0,
  match=(1),
  action=(next;)  /* east-west, kh√īng redirect */
```

`is_chassis_resident("cr-lrp-public")` l√† conditional macro ‚ÄĒ ovn-controller eval tr√™n local chassis: nŠļŅu `Chassis.name` cŠĽßa local chassis == chassis hiŠĽán sŠĽü hŠĽĮu cr port (theo `Port_Binding.chassis` cŠĽßa cr port, ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c update qua BFD/HA), return true. Khi true, packet ńĎ√£ ŠĽü ńĎ√ļng chassis n√™n `next;` ńĎi tiŠļŅp pipeline LR egress local. Khi false, ńĎŠĽēi outport sang `cr-lrp-public` ‚Üí OVN encap Geneve gŠĽ≠i tŠĽõi chassis sŠĽü hŠĽĮu cr. Invariant: sau stage n√†y, mŠĽći packet c√≥ outport l√† LRP gateway sŠļĹ kŠļŅt th√ļc tŠļ°i ńĎ√ļng 1 chassis.

**C√°ch kŠĽĻ s∆į vŠļ≠n h√†nh th√†nh thŠļ°o.** (1) **ńźŠĽćc**: `ovn-nbctl lrp-get-gateway-chassis lrp-public` xem mapping; `ovn-sbctl find Port_Binding type=chassisredirect` xem cr port ŠĽü chassis n√†o. (2) **SŠĽ≠a**: `ovn-nbctl lrp-set-gateway-chassis lrp-public chassis-1 100` + `ovn-nbctl lrp-set-gateway-chassis lrp-public chassis-2 50` (failover). (3) **Quan s√°t**: `ovn-trace lr1 'inport=="lrp-internal" && ... && ip4.dst==<external>'` xem stage 18 c√≥ redirect. (4) **Debug**: nŠļŅu N-S broken sau gateway fail, check `ovn-sbctl find Chassis_Private` xem BFD status c√°c chassis; check `ovn-sbctl get Port_Binding cr-lrp-public chassis` xem cr port c√≥ active chassis hay kh√īng.

**Ph√Ęn loŠļ°i.** LoŠļ°i stage: **gateway dispatcher** (subtype "distributed-to-centralized switch"). Kh√°c `LR_IN_DNAT` (NAT enforcement, kh√īng redirect), `LR_IN_IP_ROUTING` (route lookup, c√≥ thŠĽÉ chŠĽćn outport gateway nh∆įng kh√īng redirect). Stateless thuŠļßn.

**Quy tr√¨nh sŠĽ≠ dŠĽ•ng.**
1. TŠļ°o LR + LRP public: `ovn-nbctl lr-add lr1 && ovn-nbctl lrp-add lr1 lrp-public RR:99 1.2.3.1/24`
2. ńźńÉng k√Ĺ 2 chassis c√≥ physical bridge mapping: `ovs-vsctl set Open_vSwitch . external-ids:ovn-bridge-mappings=public:br-public` (tr√™n cŠļ£ chassis-1 v√† chassis-2)
3. Set HA gateway: `ovn-nbctl lrp-set-gateway-chassis lrp-public chassis-1 100 && ovn-nbctl lrp-set-gateway-chassis lrp-public chassis-2 50`
4. Verify cr port: `ovn-sbctl find Port_Binding type=chassisredirect` thŠļ•y `cr-lrp-public` vŠĽõi chassis = chassis-1 (priority cao nhŠļ•t)
5. Verify flow: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr1 | grep lr_in_gw_redirect` thŠļ•y flow priority 100 + 50
6. Test failover: kill ovn-controller tr√™n chassis-1 ‚Üí ńĎŠĽ£i BFD timeout (~5s) ‚Üí cr port chuyŠĽÉn sang chassis-2 ‚Üí test N-S vŠļęn work

**Khi xŠļ£y ra sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ.** Symptom: (a) "VM kh√īng truy cŠļ≠p Internet sau khi gateway chassis fail" ‚Üí step 1: kiŠĽÉm tra BFD status, step 2: nŠļŅu cr port kh√īng chuyŠĽÉn sang chassis-2, kiŠĽÉm tra HA_Chassis_Group status, step 3: nŠļŅu cr port chuyŠĽÉn nh∆įng vŠļęn fail, kiŠĽÉm tra physical bridge mapping tr√™n chassis-2. (b) "Sau gateway chassis fail, c√≥ 5s loss" ‚Üí BFD interval default 1000ms √ó 5 = 5s; c√≥ thŠĽÉ giŠļ£m xuŠĽĎng 200ms √ó 3 = 600ms. (c) "Gateway chassis CPU 100% nh∆įng cluster c√≥ 5 chassis" ‚Üí gateway centralize ŠĽü 1 chassis l√† bottleneck cho tŠĽēng N-S traffic; consider th√™m `Logical_Router_Port` ri√™ng cho mŠĽói chassis (multi-gw pattern OVN 23.06+). Cross-link: PhŠļßn 13.6 ¬ßHA chassis group + BFD, PhŠļßn 13.18 ¬ßREGBIT_NAT_REDIRECT.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** Tightly coupled: `Logical_Router_Port.gateway_chassis` (NBDB nguŠĽďn dŠĽĮ liŠĽáu), `HA_Chassis_Group` + `HA_Chassis` (HA election), `Port_Binding.type=chassisredirect` (cr port virtual), `BFD` table (link liveness), `is_chassis_resident()` predicate, `LR_IN_ARP_RESOLVE` (stage tr∆įŠĽõc resolve next-hop), `LR_OUT_DELIVERY` (stage egress sau redirect). Loose: ovn-bridge-mappings (config OVS b√™n d∆įŠĽõi, kh√īng phŠļ£i NBDB).

**Kh√°c biŠĽát giŠĽĮa c√°c phi√™n bŠļ£n.**
- OVN 2.10 (2018): chŠĽČ centralized gateway router, kh√īng c√≥ chassisredirect concept
- OVN 21.06 (2021): introduce distributed gateway + cr port + stage n√†y
- OVN 22.03 (2022): integrate HA_Chassis_Group cho HA failover qua BFD
- OVN 23.06 (2023): `redirect-type=bridged` alternative (qua LS thay Geneve)
- OVN 24.03 (2024): tŠĽĎi ∆įu skip redirect cho LB DNAT khi target VM c√Ļng hypervisor

**C√°ch quan s√°t + x√°c minh.**

```
$ ovn-nbctl lrp-get-gateway-chassis lrp-public
  chassis-1   100
  chassis-2   50

$ ovn-sbctl find Port_Binding type=chassisredirect
  _uuid               : abc-...
  logical_port        : "cr-lrp-public"
  chassis             : [chassis-1-uuid]   /* active chassis */
  type                : chassisredirect

$ ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr1 | grep "lr_in_gw_redirect"
  table=18 (lr_in_gw_redirect), priority=100,
    match=(outport == "lrp-public" && !is_chassis_resident("cr-lrp-public")),
    action=(outport = "cr-lrp-public"; next;)

$ ovn-trace lr1 'inport=="lrp-internal" && eth.dst==RR:11 && ip4 && ip4.src==10.0.0.5 && ip4.dst==8.8.8.8'
  ‚Üí ingress(dp="lr1", inport="lrp-internal")
    16. lr_in_arp_resolve ‚Üí resolve next-hop MAC
    18. lr_in_gw_redirect (priority=100, !is_chassis_resident)
        outport = "cr-lrp-public";
        next;
```

**Source code.** Tham chiŠļŅu OVN branch-22.03:
- `northd/northd.c` `build_gateway_redirect_flows_for_lrouter()`: h√†m ch√≠nh build stage n√†y
- `northd/northd.c` `build_gateway_redirect_flows_for_lrouter_port()`: per-LRP build
- `controller/binding.c` `consider_local_datapath()`: xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ chassisredirect Port_Binding
- `controller/ha-chassis.c` `ha_chassis_group_run()`: HA election logic
- `lib/lflow.h` `S_ROUTER_IN_GW_REDIRECT = 18`: stage id

**Tr∆įŠĽĚng hŠĽ£p sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ.** Q3/2024 production: customer b√°o "sau khi reboot chassis-1 (gateway chassis primary), tenant N-S broken 30 gi√Ęy thay v√¨ <5s expected". Investigation: BFD timeout ńĎ√ļng 5s (config interval=1000 multiplier=5). Sau BFD down, OVN northd phŠļ£i re-compile flow (cr port chuyŠĽÉn chassis), ovn-controller c√°c chassis c√≤n lŠļ°i nhŠļ≠n update SBDB. ńźo `ovn-sbctl get Port_Binding cr-lrp-public chassis` thŠļ•y update chŠĽČ sau ~3s. Nh∆įng test traffic vŠļęn drop tŠĽõi ~30s. Root cause: ARP cache tr√™n switch physical b√™n ngo√†i cluster vŠļęn trŠĽŹ MAC chassis-1 (gateway physical interface MAC). CŠļßn GARP tŠĽę chassis-2 advertise IP cŠĽßa LRP public sang c√Ļng physical network. OVN c√≥ gŠĽ≠i GARP nh∆įng switch upstream l√ļc ńĎ√≥ throttle GARP (storm protection). Fix: tńÉng `Logical_Router_Port.options:ra_arp_rate_limit` ńĎŠĽÉ cŠĽ•m GARP nhiŠĽĀu lŠļßn; hoŠļ∑c y√™u cŠļßu network team disable GARP throttle tr√™n switch. Cross-link PhŠļßn 13.18 ¬ßREGBIT_NAT_REDIRECT.

**B√†i tŠļ≠p synthetic.**

```bash
sudo ovn-nbctl lr-add lr-lab
sudo ovn-nbctl lrp-add lr-lab lrp-internal RR:11 10.0.0.1/24
sudo ovn-nbctl lrp-add lr-lab lrp-public RR:99 1.2.3.1/24
sudo ovn-nbctl lrp-set-gateway-chassis lrp-public chassis-1 100
sudo ovn-nbctl lrp-set-gateway-chassis lrp-public chassis-2 50
# Lab task 1: ovn-trace tŠĽę vm tŠĽõi external 8.8.8.8 ‚Üí verify stage 18 redirect tŠĽõi cr-lrp-public
# Lab task 2: ovn-sbctl find Port_Binding type=chassisredirect ‚Üí verify chassis hiŠĽán active = chassis-1
# Lab task 3: stop ovn-controller tr√™n chassis-1 ‚Üí ńĎŠĽ£i 5s ‚Üí verify cr port chuyŠĽÉn chassis-2
# Lab task 4: bŠļ≠t lŠļ°i chassis-1 ‚Üí verify cr port quay vŠĽĀ chassis-1 (priority 100 cao h∆°n)
# Lab task 5: ńĎŠĽēi gateway_chassis priority chassis-2 l√™n 200 ‚Üí verify cr port chuyŠĽÉn ngay
```

**LŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p + t√≠n hiŠĽáu chŠļ©n ńĎo√°n.**
- Mode A "cr port stuck ŠĽü chassis fail": HA_Chassis_Group election broken ‚Üí check BFD status + chassis-private records
- Mode B "Failover chŠļ≠m": BFD interval/multiplier qu√° lŠĽõn ‚Üí giŠļ£m ńĎŠĽÉ < 1s
- Mode C "Sau failover, packet vŠļęn rŠĽõt": ARP cache upstream switch stale ‚Üí tńÉng GARP rate hoŠļ∑c reset network upstream
- Mode D "Gateway chassis CPU 100%": tŠļ•t cŠļ£ N-S qua 1 chassis ‚Üí consider multi-LR pattern hoŠļ∑c redirect-type=bridged
- Mode E "redirect kh√īng xŠļ£y ra": LRP ch∆įa c√≥ gateway_chassis config ‚Üí set qua lrp-set-gateway-chassis

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Cisco HSRP/VRRP gateway redundancy t∆į∆°ng tŠĽĪ √Ĺ t∆įŠĽüng (active/standby gateway, virtual MAC) nh∆įng OVN d√Ļng BFD + chassisredirect pattern kh√°c: OVN kh√īng c√≥ virtual MAC chia sŠļĽ, m√† l√† chuyŠĽÉn ńĎ∆įŠĽĚng packet qua tunnel sang chassis active. NSX-T edge cluster vŠĽõi "service router" centralized analog: c√Ļng chia th√†nh DR distributed + SR centralized, gateway service centralize ŠĽü edge node. Linux keepalived + VIP analog: VIP migration giŠĽĮa node, nh∆įng layer thŠļ•p h∆°n (kh√īng c√≥ pipeline overlay). AWS NAT Gateway managed service (centralize per-AZ) t∆į∆°ng ńĎ∆į∆°ng semantic.

## ¬ß13.19.11 LS_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK ‚ÄĒ KiŠĽÉm tra session affinity cho Load Balancer

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LS_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK` l√† stage logic ingress LS thŠĽĪc hiŠĽán **lookup** bŠļ£ng `OVN_Southbound.MAC_Binding`-style affinity ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c l∆įu trong conntrack zone phŠĽ• (Affinity zone) ńĎŠĽÉ ph√°t hiŠĽán mŠĽôt client ńĎ√£ tŠĽęng ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c g√°n cho backend n√†o tr∆įŠĽõc ńĎ√≥. NŠļŅu tr√Ļng (sticky hit), stage set `REGBIT_KNOWN_LB_SESSION = 1` v√† bypass thŠļ≥ng tŠĽõi `LS_IN_LB` vŠĽõi backend ńĎ√£ learn (kh√īng hash lŠļ°i). NŠļŅu miss, packet ńĎi tiŠļŅp tŠĽõi `LS_IN_LB` ńĎŠĽÉ hash chŠĽćn backend mŠĽõi v√† sau ńĎ√≥ stage `LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` ghi hŠĽćc. LoŠļ°i stage: **stateful pre-LB lookup** dŠļ°ng cornerstone phŠĽ• (medium importance), sub-loŠļ°i "session affinity matcher".

**LŠĽčch sŠĽ≠ + bŠĽĎi cŠļ£nh.** OVN 22.09 giŠĽõi thiŠĽáu `LR_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` cho Logical Router LB affinity. OVN 23.03 mŠĽü rŠĽông cho Logical Switch (th√™m `LS_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK` ŠĽü vŠĽč tr√≠ stage 11 tr√™n LS pipeline) ńĎ√°p ŠĽ©ng y√™u cŠļßu Octavia OVN provider sticky-session ŠĽü east-west traffic. OVN 23.06 ńĎŠļ©y stage CHECK l√™n vŠĽč tr√≠ 12 (sau khi pipeline ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c t√°i sŠļĮp xŠļŅp giŠĽĮa PRE_STATEFUL v√† LB). T√≠nh nńÉng dŠĽĪa tr√™n `Load_Balancer.options:affinity_timeout` (gi√° trŠĽč gi√Ęy, mŠļ∑c ńĎŠĽčnh 0 = disabled). Tr∆įŠĽõc affinity stage, sticky chŠĽČ ńĎŠļ°t ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c qua `selection_fields` hash-based (kh√īng ch√≠nh x√°c khi tŠļ≠p backend thay ńĎŠĽēi). Curriculum b√°m 22.03 baseline nh∆įng note r√Ķ stage CHECK xuŠļ•t hiŠĽán ŠĽü 23.03+.

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Trong OVN 23.06+, stage sŠĽĎ 12 (OF table 14 tr√™n br-int sau offset 8). ńźŠĽ©ng tr∆įŠĽõc `LS_IN_LB` (stage 13) v√† sau `LS_IN_QOS_METER` (stage 10). Scope: per-packet per-datapath. Li√™n kŠļŅt vŠĽõi conntrack zone affinity ri√™ng biŠĽát (`reg11`) kh√°c zone cŠĽßa LB DNAT.

**Vai tr√≤.** ńźŠļ£m bŠļ£o c√Ļng mŠĽôt client (nguŠĽďn IP, hoŠļ∑c nguŠĽďn IP + nguŠĽďn port tuŠĽ≥ `affinity_timeout` config) li√™n tŠĽ•c ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c route ńĎŠļŅn c√Ļng mŠĽôt backend trong khoŠļ£ng thŠĽĚi gian sticky. PhŠļ°m vi vai tr√≤: chŠĽČ kiŠĽÉm tra (read-only ńĎŠĽĎi vŠĽõi conntrack); viŠĽác commit hŠĽćc bŠĽč t√°ch qua stage `LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` xuŠĽĎng d∆įŠĽõi ‚ÄĒ pattern check-then-learn cŠĽē ńĎiŠĽÉn.

**V√¨ sao sinh ra.** Tr∆įŠĽõc affinity stage, OVN sticky session phŠļ£i dŠĽĪa v√†o `selection_fields=ip_src` hash-based. Nh∆įng hash mod N_backend kh√īng ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh khi N thay ńĎŠĽēi (backend scale-up/down): c√Ļng client c√≥ thŠĽÉ map ńĎŠļŅn backend kh√°c nhau g√Ęy mŠļ•t session. `affinity_timeout` + 2 stage CHECK/LEARN l∆įu trŠĽĮ explicit mapping client‚Üíbackend trong conntrack table affinity zone, sŠĽĎng ńĎ√ļng `affinity_timeout` gi√Ęy, ho√†n to√†n ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh tr∆įŠĽõc thay ńĎŠĽēi backend list.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** CŠĽ• thŠĽÉ: sticky session vŠĽõi (a) ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh tr∆įŠĽõc scale, (b) timeout c√≥ thŠĽÉ cŠļ•u h√¨nh per-LB (kh√īng chung global), (c) granularity client-IP hoŠļ∑c client-IP-port (per-flow). C√°ch giŠļ£i: stage CHECK emit `ct(table=Next, zone=affinity_zone, nat)` ńĎŠĽÉ probe affinity entry; nŠļŅu match, h√†nh ńĎŠĽông `next` skip qua LB hash. NŠļŅu kh√īng, ńĎi tiŠļŅp `LS_IN_LB` chŠĽćn backend qua hash, rŠĽďi `LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` commit affinity entry v√†o zone affinity vŠĽõi expire = `affinity_timeout`. PhŠļ°m vi: chŠĽČ √°p dŠĽ•ng khi VIP c√≥ `Load_Balancer.options:affinity_timeout > 0`.

**TŠļßm quan trŠĽćng.** MŠĽ©c trung b√¨nh. CŠļßn thiŠļŅt cho workload y√™u cŠļßu strict sticky (v√≠ dŠĽ•: web app login session, gRPC long-lived stream vŠĽõi state per-backend). Octavia OVN provider sŠĽ≠ dŠĽ•ng ńĎŠĽÉ bridge gap vŠĽõi HAProxy `cookie`-based sticky. Engineer cloud network cŠļßn biŠļŅt khi n√†o enable affinity thay v√¨ chŠĽČ hash-based.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** `build_lb_affinity_ls_flows` trong `northd/northd.c` (verified branch-23.06+) sinh c√°c flow sau cho mŠĽói VIP c√≥ `affinity_timeout > 0`:

```
table=12 (ls_in_lb_aff_check), priority=100,
  match=(ct.new && ip4 && reg9[6] == 0 && ip4.dst == 10.0.0.100 && tcp.dst == 80),
  action=(reg9[6] = 1; ct_lb_mark(backends=...);)

table=12 (ls_in_lb_aff_check), priority=150,
  match=(ct.new && ip4 && reg9[6] == 1 && ip4.dst == 10.0.0.100 && tcp.dst == 80
         && ip4.src == <learned_client>),
  action=(/* skip hash, go directly to learned backend */
          ct_lb_mark(backends=<learned_backend>);)

table=12 (ls_in_lb_aff_check), priority=0,
  match=(1), action=(next;)
```

CŠĽĚ `reg9[6]` (`REGBIT_KNOWN_LB_SESSION`) d√Ļng ńĎŠĽÉ branch giŠĽĮa hai nh√°nh sticky-hit v√† sticky-miss. Backend ńĎ√£ learn ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c l∆įu trong affinity conntrack entry; lookup match qua `ct_state` cŠĽßa zone affinity ri√™ng biŠĽát (zone ńĎŠĽčnh nghń©a qua `Load_Balancer.options:affinity_timeout`).

**C√°ch kŠĽĻ s∆į vŠļ≠n h√†nh th√†nh thŠļ°o.** (1) **ńźŠĽćc**: hiŠĽÉu ph√Ęn biŠĽát CHECK vs LEARN, hai stage bŠĽē trŠĽ£ nhau. (2) **SŠĽ≠a**: `ovn-nbctl --wait=hv set Load_Balancer lb-web options:affinity_timeout=300` (5 ph√ļt sticky). (3) **Quan s√°t**: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<aff_zone>` xem entry sticky. (4) **Debug**: `ovn-trace` packet client ‚Üí VIP, xem stage CHECK match priority 150 hay 100 ńĎŠĽÉ biŠļŅt hit hay miss.

**Ph√Ęn loŠļ°i.** LoŠļ°i stage: **affinity matcher** (subtype "stateful sticky lookup"). Kh√°c `LS_IN_LB` (hash-based selection), kh√°c `LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` (write-side sibling), kh√°c `LR_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK` (router-side analog cho north-south LB).

**Quy tr√¨nh sŠĽ≠ dŠĽ•ng.**
1. TŠļ°o LB: `ovn-nbctl lb-add lb-web "10.0.0.100:80" "10.0.0.5:80,10.0.0.6:80"`
2. BŠļ≠t affinity: `ovn-nbctl set Load_Balancer lb-web options:affinity_timeout=180`
3. GŠļĮn v√†o LS: `ovn-nbctl ls-lb-add ls1 lb-web`
4. Verify compile: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls1 | grep "ls_in_lb_aff_check"` thŠļ•y 2-3 flow priority 100/150/0
5. Test sticky: client gŠĽ≠i 10 request li√™n tiŠļŅp ńĎŠļŅn VIP ‚Üí 100% ńĎŠļŅn c√Ļng 1 backend (trong 180 gi√Ęy)
6. Test scale: th√™m backend thŠĽ© 3 ‚Üí client cŇ© vŠļęn sticky ńĎŠļŅn backend cŇ©; client mŠĽõi c√≥ thŠĽÉ chŠĽćn backend mŠĽõi

**Khi xŠļ£y ra sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ.** Symptom: "ńĎ√£ set affinity_timeout=300 nh∆įng client vŠļęn rotate backend mŠĽói request". Diagnostic step-by-step:
- Step 1: `ovn-nbctl get Load_Balancer lb-web options:affinity_timeout` x√°c nhŠļ≠n gi√° trŠĽč > 0
- Step 2: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls1 | grep ls_in_lb_aff_check` xem c√≥ flow priority 150 kh√īng (nŠļŅu kh√īng c√≥, OVN version ch∆įa hŠĽó trŠĽ£ LS affinity ‚Üí upgrade ‚Č• 23.03)
- Step 3: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack | grep <client_ip>` xem entry zone affinity c√≥ tŠĽďn tŠļ°i kh√īng; nŠļŅu kh√īng, c√≥ thŠĽÉ conntrack zone bŠĽč reset bŠĽüi service restart
- Step 4: kiŠĽÉm tra `ovn-trace` packet ńĎŠĽÉ x√°c ńĎŠĽčnh stage CHECK match priority n√†o

Cross-link PhŠļßn 13.9 ¬ßLB affinity timeout, PhŠļßn 13.18 ¬ßREGBIT_KNOWN_LB_SESSION.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** Tightly coupled: `LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` (write-side sibling), `LS_IN_LB` (downstream hash fallback), `Load_Balancer.options:affinity_timeout` (config trigger), `reg9[6]` REGBIT_KNOWN_LB_SESSION, conntrack zone affinity. Loose: `LR_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK` (LR analog), `LS_IN_PRE_LB` (zone setup chung).

**Kh√°c biŠĽát giŠĽĮa c√°c phi√™n bŠļ£n.**
- OVN 22.03 (baseline): ch∆įa c√≥ stage n√†y. Sticky chŠĽČ qua `selection_fields` hash.
- OVN 22.09: introduce LR-side `LR_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` cho north-south LB.
- OVN 23.03: introduce `LS_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK` ŠĽü stage 11 (c√Ļng `LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN`).
- OVN 23.06: re-order, CHECK ŠĽü stage 12, LEARN ŠĽü stage 14, LB ŠĽü stage 13 giŠĽĮa.
- OVN 24.03+: ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh, th√™m `Load_Balancer.options:hairpin_orig_tuple` integration.

**C√°ch quan s√°t + x√°c minh.**

```
$ ovn-nbctl set Load_Balancer lb-web options:affinity_timeout=120
$ ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls1 | grep -A2 "ls_in_lb_aff_check"
  table=12 (ls_in_lb_aff_check), priority=100,
    match=(ct.new && ip4 && reg9[6] == 0 && ip4.dst == 10.0.0.100 && tcp.dst == 80),
    action=(reg9[6] = 1;)
  table=12 (ls_in_lb_aff_check), priority=150,
    match=(... && ip4.src == 10.0.0.20 && reg9[6] == 1),
    action=(... go to learned backend ...)

$ ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack | grep "zone=<aff>" | head -3
  tcp,orig=(src=10.0.0.20,...), zone=<aff_zone>, mark=<backend_idx>
```

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.**
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lb_affinity_ls_flows()`: h√†m ch√≠nh sinh flow CHECK + LEARN cho LS (verified branch-23.06)
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lswitch_lb_affinity_default_flows()`: priority-0 default flow
- `northd/northd.h` `S_SWITCH_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK = 12` (branch-23.06 PIPELINE_STAGES)
- `controller/lflow.c` dŠĽčch `ct_lb_mark` xuŠĽĎng OVS `ct(commit, mark=...)`
- `lib/actions.c` parser cho `ct_lb_mark` vŠĽõi affinity zone

**Tr∆įŠĽĚng hŠĽ£p sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ.** Q3/2024 production Octavia OVN provider: customer report "user login phŠļ£i lŠļ∑p lŠļ°i sau ~30 gi√Ęy mŠļ∑c d√Ļ ńĎ√£ set affinity_timeout=600". Investigation: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls-frontend | grep ls_in_lb_aff_check` chŠĽČ thŠļ•y flow priority 0 (default), kh√īng c√≥ priority 100/150 ‚ÄĒ nghń©a l√† OVN kh√īng sinh affinity flows. Root cause: `ovn-northd` ńĎang chŠļ°y version 22.09 (ch∆įa hŠĽó trŠĽ£ LS affinity, chŠĽČ LR), trong khi LB attached v√†o LS thay v√¨ LR. Fix: upgrade l√™n OVN 23.06 hoŠļ∑c detach LB rŠĽďi attach lŠļ°i v√†o LR thay v√¨ LS. Cross-link PhŠļßn 13.9 ¬ßLB version-specific.

**B√†i tŠļ≠p synthetic.**

```bash
sudo ovn-nbctl ls-add ls-aff
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-aff lsp-client
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-aff lsp-be1
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-aff lsp-be2
sudo ovn-nbctl lb-add lb-sticky "10.0.0.100:80" "10.0.0.5:80,10.0.0.6:80"

sudo ovn-nbctl ls-lb-add ls-aff lb-sticky
# Lab task 1: gŠĽ≠i 5 request tŠĽę client (c√Ļng src_ip src_port) ‚Üí ńĎŠļŅm sŠĽĎ lŠļßn tŠĽõi mŠĽói backend (kŠĽ≥ vŠĽćng 100% 1 backend)
# Lab task 2: gŠĽ≠i 5 request mŠĽõi vŠĽõi src_port kh√°c (vŠļęn c√Ļng src_ip) ‚Üí vŠļęn 100% 1 backend
# Lab task 3: ńĎŠĽ£i > 120s ‚Üí gŠĽ≠i lŠļ°i ‚Üí c√≥ thŠĽÉ chuyŠĽÉn backend kh√°c
# Lab task 4: th√™m backend thŠĽ© 3, client cŇ© vŠļęn sticky backend cŇ©
```

**LŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p + t√≠n hiŠĽáu chŠļ©n ńĎo√°n.**
- Mode A "kh√īng c√≥ flow CHECK": OVN version < 23.03 hoŠļ∑c LB attached LR thay v√¨ LS ‚Üí upgrade hoŠļ∑c t√°i attach
- Mode B "sticky timeout kh√īng ńĎ√ļng": `affinity_timeout` set qu√° ngŠļĮn so vŠĽõi session lifetime ‚Üí tńÉng gi√° trŠĽč
- Mode C "sticky bŠĽč mŠļ•t sau service restart": conntrack zone affinity flush khi ovs-vswitchd restart ‚Üí expected behaviour, document cho user
- Mode D "sticky √°p dŠĽ•ng kh√īng mong muŠĽĎn": LB share giŠĽĮa nhiŠĽĀu LS, affinity_timeout √°p to√†n bŠĽô ‚Üí t√°ch LB ri√™ng cho tŠĽęng LS

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** HAProxy `cookie SERVERID insert` cookie-based sticky analog (layer 7, kh√īng cŠļßn conntrack). NGINX `sticky cookie` t∆į∆°ng tŠĽĪ HAProxy. Cisco ACE `sticky http-cookie` c√Ļng family. AWS ALB `stickiness.enabled=true` cookie-based. Linux IPVS `--persistent` analog gŠļßn nhŠļ•t ŠĽü L4 (IP-based sticky). Kh√°c: OVN affinity l√† conntrack-based stateful trong kernel datapath OVS, latency thŠļ•p h∆°n cookie-based L7.

---

## ¬ß13.19.12 LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN ‚ÄĒ HŠĽćc mapping client‚Üíbackend cho session affinity

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` l√† stage logic ingress LS **ghi** v√†o affinity conntrack zone mapping (client_ip[:client_port]) ‚Üí (backend_ip:port) sau khi `LS_IN_LB` ńĎ√£ chŠĽćn backend mŠĽõi qua hash. Mapping sŠĽĎng ńĎ√ļng `affinity_timeout` gi√Ęy, sau ńĎ√≥ tŠĽĪ expire. Stage chŠļ°y sau LB v√† tr∆įŠĽõc PRE_HAIRPIN. LoŠļ°i: **stateful sticky writer** (medium importance), sub-loŠļ°i "affinity entry committer".

**LŠĽčch sŠĽ≠ + bŠĽĎi cŠļ£nh.** OVN 22.09 introduce `LR_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` cho LR. OVN 23.03 th√™m `LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` cho LS (c√Ļng `LS_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK`). OVN 23.06 ńĎŠļ©y stage l√™n vŠĽč tr√≠ 14 (sau LB stage 13). T√°ch CHECK + LEARN th√†nh 2 stage l√† pattern lookup-then-commit cŠĽē ńĎiŠĽÉn: CHECK lookup rŠĽďi nŠļŅu miss th√¨ stage LB chŠĽćn, rŠĽďi LEARN commit kŠļŅt quŠļ£.

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Trong OVN 23.06+, stage sŠĽĎ 14 (OF table 16). ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LS_IN_LB` (stage 13) v√† tr∆įŠĽõc `LS_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN` (stage 15). Scope: per-packet per-datapath. T∆į∆°ng t√°c vŠĽõi c√Ļng affinity zone cŠĽßa CHECK stage.

**Vai tr√≤.** Persist mapping ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c tŠļ°o bŠĽüi LB hash th√†nh affinity entry ńĎŠĽÉ CHECK stage t∆į∆°ng lai c√≥ thŠĽÉ match (sticky hit). PhŠļ°m vi vai tr√≤: write-only, kh√īng tham gia routing decision cŠĽßa packet hiŠĽán tŠļ°i ‚ÄĒ packet hiŠĽán tŠļ°i ńĎ√£ ńĎi ńĎ∆įŠĽĚng LB hash xong; LEARN chŠĽČ ghi nhŠĽõ cho packet sau.

**V√¨ sao sinh ra.** CŠļßn mŠĽôt stage ri√™ng ńĎŠĽÉ commit affinity v√¨: (a) commit chŠĽČ thŠĽĪc hiŠĽán khi `reg9[6]==0` (sticky-miss path, kh√īng cŠļßn re-commit khi hit); (b) commit phŠļ£i xŠļ£y ra sau khi backend ńĎ√£ ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c hash chŠĽćn (sau LS_IN_LB); (c) commit d√Ļng action `commit_lb_aff` ri√™ng biŠĽát vŠĽõi conntrack zone affinity, kh√īng tr√Ļng vŠĽõi `ct(commit)` cŠĽßa LB DNAT zone. T√°ch stage gi√ļp tr√°nh phŠĽ©c tŠļ°p lŠĽďng action v√†o LS_IN_LB.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** CŠĽ• thŠĽÉ: l∆įu trŠĽĮ persistent mapping client‚Üíbackend vŠĽõi expire timer per-entry, kh√īng phŠĽ• thuŠĽôc v√†o lifetime cŠĽßa TCP connection ch√≠nh (entry sŠĽĎng ńĎŠĽôc lŠļ≠p). C√°ch giŠļ£i: sau LB hash xong, action `commit_lb_aff(vip=..., backend=..., timeout=<affinity_timeout>)` ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c emit; controller dŠĽčch xuŠĽĎng OVS `ct(commit, zone=<aff>, exec(set_field:<backend>->ct_label))` c√Ļng `learn` action gŠļĮn timeout. PhŠļ°m vi: chŠĽČ packet `ct.new` ńĎi qua sticky-miss path.

**TŠļßm quan trŠĽćng.** MŠĽ©c trung b√¨nh. BŠļĮt buŠĽôc phŠļ£i c√≥ khi VIP enable affinity_timeout, nŠļŅu kh√īng CHECK stage sŠļĹ lu√īn miss (kh√īng c√≥ entry n√†o ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c hŠĽćc) ‚Üí sticky g√£y. Engineer cŠļßn debug LEARN stage khi sticky kh√īng hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông ŠĽü packet thŠĽ© 2 trŠĽü ńĎi.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** `build_lb_affinity_ls_flows` (verified branch-23.06+ `northd/northd.c`) sinh flow LEARN t∆į∆°ng ŠĽ©ng vŠĽõi mŠĽói VIP affinity:

```
table=14 (ls_in_lb_aff_learn), priority=100,
  match=(ct.new && ip4 && reg9[6] == 0 && ip4.dst == 10.0.0.100 && tcp.dst == 80),
  action=(commit_lb_aff(vip = "10.0.0.100:80",
                        backend = "10.0.0.5:80",
                        timeout = 180);)

table=14 (ls_in_lb_aff_learn), priority=0,
  match=(1), action=(next;)
```

Action `commit_lb_aff` ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c parser `lib/actions.c` parse rŠĽďi controller dŠĽčch xuŠĽĎng OVS sequence: `ct(commit, zone=<aff_zone>), set_field:<backend_idx>->ct_label[0..7], set_field:<timeout>->ct_label[8..23]`. Khi entry expire, kernel conntrack tŠĽĪ xo√°; CHECK stage t∆į∆°ng lai lookup miss ‚Üí hash lŠļ°i.

**C√°ch kŠĽĻ s∆į vŠļ≠n h√†nh th√†nh thŠļ°o.** (1) **ńźŠĽćc**: hiŠĽÉu CHECK vs LEARN t√°ch biŠĽát; LEARN chŠĽČ chŠļ°y ŠĽü sticky-miss path. (2) **SŠĽ≠a**: c√Ļng config vŠĽõi CHECK qua `affinity_timeout` option. (3) **Quan s√°t**: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<aff>` xem entry mŠĽõi ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c hŠĽćc sau request ńĎŠļßu ti√™n. (4) **Debug**: nŠļŅu sticky g√£y, kiŠĽÉm tra LEARN flow priority 100 c√≥ khŠĽõp packet kh√īng qua `ovn-trace`.

**Ph√Ęn loŠļ°i.** LoŠļ°i stage: **affinity writer** (subtype "stateful sticky committer"). Kh√°c `LS_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK` (read-side sibling), kh√°c `LS_IN_STATEFUL` (commit conntrack DNAT zone), kh√°c `LR_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` (LR analog).

**Quy tr√¨nh sŠĽ≠ dŠĽ•ng.** TŠĽĪ ńĎŠĽông hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông khi `affinity_timeout > 0`. Kh√īng cŠļßn config ri√™ng cho LEARN. Quy tr√¨nh kiŠĽÉm chŠĽ©ng:
1. Set affinity_timeout (xem stage CHECK ¬ß13.19.11)
2. GŠĽ≠i request ńĎŠļßu ti√™n tŠĽę client ‚Üí LEARN stage commit entry
3. `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<aff>` thŠļ•y entry mŠĽõi
4. GŠĽ≠i request thŠĽ© 2 ‚Üí CHECK stage hit, kh√īng commit lŠļ°i
5. ńźŠĽ£i ńĎŠļŅn qu√° `affinity_timeout` ‚Üí entry expire ‚Üí CHECK miss ‚Üí LEARN commit lŠļ°i

**Khi xŠļ£y ra sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ.** Symptom: "request ńĎŠļßu sticky ńĎ√ļng nh∆įng request 2 trŠĽü ńĎi rotate". Diagnostic:
- Step 1: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<aff> | grep <client>` x√°c nhŠļ≠n entry tŠĽďn tŠļ°i sau request 1
- Step 2: nŠļŅu entry kh√īng xuŠļ•t hiŠĽán, kiŠĽÉm tra LEARN flow priority 100 qua `ovn-sbctl lflow-list`
- Step 3: nŠļŅu flow tŠĽďn tŠļ°i nh∆įng entry kh√īng l∆įu, kernel conntrack module c√≥ thŠĽÉ bŠĽč disable ‚Üí `lsmod | grep nf_conntrack`
- Step 4: nŠļŅu zone full hoŠļ∑c entry bŠĽč purge sŠĽõm, kiŠĽÉm tra `nf_conntrack_max` v√† xem c√°c entry c√≥ bŠĽč evict do LRU kh√īng

Cross-link PhŠļßn 13.9 ¬ßaffinity zone, PhŠļßn 13.18 ¬ßcommit_lb_aff action.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** Tightly coupled: `LS_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK` (read-side sibling), `LS_IN_LB` (upstream chŠĽćn backend), action `commit_lb_aff`, conntrack zone affinity, `Load_Balancer.options:affinity_timeout`. Loose: `LR_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN` (LR analog).

**Kh√°c biŠĽát giŠĽĮa c√°c phi√™n bŠļ£n.**
- OVN 22.03: ch∆įa c√≥ stage n√†y
- OVN 22.09: introduce LR-side LEARN cho north-south
- OVN 23.03: introduce LS-side LEARN ŠĽü stage 11 (c√Ļng CHECK)
- OVN 23.06+: re-order, LEARN ŠĽü stage 14 (sau LB stage 13)

**C√°ch quan s√°t + x√°c minh.**

```
$ ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls1 | grep -A2 "ls_in_lb_aff_learn"
  table=14 (ls_in_lb_aff_learn), priority=100,
    match=(ct.new && reg9[6] == 0 && ip4.dst == 10.0.0.100 && tcp.dst == 80),
    action=(commit_lb_aff(vip="10.0.0.100:80", backend="10.0.0.5:80", timeout=180);)

$ ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<aff_zone>
  tcp,orig=(src=10.0.0.20,sport=*,dst=10.0.0.100,dport=80),
       mark=0, labels=0x0001b40000000000,  # backend_idx=0, timeout=180
       zone=<aff_zone>, expiry=178s
```

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.**
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lb_affinity_ls_flows()`: chung cho cŠļ£ CHECK v√† LEARN
- `lib/actions.c` parser `parse_commit_lb_aff()` cho action `commit_lb_aff`
- `controller/lflow.c` dŠĽčch `commit_lb_aff` xuŠĽĎng OVS `ct(commit, zone=<aff>) + set_field`
- `northd/northd.h` `S_SWITCH_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN = 14` (branch-23.06)

**Tr∆įŠĽĚng hŠĽ£p sŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ.** Q4/2024 staging environment: customer test sticky session, request 1 ńĎ√ļng backend, request 2 ńĎŠļŅn backend kh√°c. Investigation: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<aff>` empty sau request 1. Root cause: `Load_Balancer.options:affinity_timeout=180s` ńĎ√£ set nh∆įng `ovn-northd` ńĎ√£ reload pre-empt khi c√≥ schema change parallel kh√°c ‚Üí flow LEARN priority 100 thiŠļŅu trong v√≤ng v√†i gi√Ęy. Fix: set lŠļ°i affinity_timeout trigger northd full re-compile + verify flow xuŠļ•t hiŠĽán tr∆įŠĽõc khi test sticky. Cross-link PhŠļßn 13.9 ¬ßaffinity timing.

**B√†i tŠļ≠p synthetic.**

```bash
# TiŠĽĀn ńĎiŠĽĀu kiŠĽán: lab task LS_IN_LB_AFF_CHECK ńĎ√£ setup
# Lab task 1: clear conntrack zone aff ‚Üí verify entry trŠĽĎng
sudo ovs-appctl dpctl/flush-conntrack zone=<aff_zone>
# Lab task 2: gŠĽ≠i 1 request tŠĽę client ‚Üí ngay sau ńĎ√≥ dump-conntrack zone aff ‚Üí verify entry mŠĽõi
sudo ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<aff_zone> | grep <client_ip>
# Lab task 3: ńĎŠĽ£i ńĎ√ļng (affinity_timeout - 5)s ‚Üí entry vŠļęn c√≤n
# Lab task 4: ńĎŠĽ£i tiŠļŅp 10s nŠĽĮa (v∆įŠĽ£t timeout) ‚Üí entry mŠļ•t ‚Üí request mŠĽõi c√≥ thŠĽÉ chŠĽćn backend kh√°c
# Lab task 5: stress test 1000 client distinct ‚Üí ńĎŠļŅm sŠĽĎ entry, kh√īng v∆įŠĽ£t nf_conntrack_max
```

**LŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p + t√≠n hiŠĽáu chŠļ©n ńĎo√°n.**
- Mode A "entry kh√īng ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c hŠĽćc": LEARN flow thiŠļŅu (northd version cŇ©) hoŠļ∑c kernel conntrack module disable
- Mode B "entry expire qu√° nhanh": `affinity_timeout` < TCP keepalive ‚Üí entry expire trong khi connection vŠļęn idle ‚Üí tńÉng affinity_timeout ‚Č• keepalive
- Mode C "zone full early": affinity zone share vŠĽõi DNAT zone ‚Üí xung ńĎŠĽôt ‚Üí t√°ch zone qua northd config (default ńĎ√£ t√°ch)
- Mode D "entry hŠĽćc sai backend": race condition giŠĽĮa CHECK miss v√† LB hash + LEARN commit khi backend list thay ńĎŠĽēi giŠĽĮa stage ‚Üí hiŠļŅm nh∆įng c√≥ thŠĽÉ xŠļ£y ra; mitigate qua quiesce period khi remove backend

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** HAProxy `cookie SERVERID insert indirect` analog (commit-side, ghi cookie sau LB chŠĽćn server). NGINX `sticky cookie srv_id ...` c√Ļng pattern. Linux IPVS `--persistent`: timeout-based learning gŠļßn nhŠļ•t. Cisco ACE `sticky` config persistent-rebalance similar. AWS ALB target-stickiness duration-based analog.

---

## ¬ß13.19.13 LS_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN ‚ÄĒ Ph√°t hiŠĽán hairpin LB (client = backend c√Ļng LSP)

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LS_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN` l√† stage logic ingress LS ph√°t hiŠĽán scenario **hairpin**: mŠĽôt LSP (cŠĽ• thŠĽÉ l√† VM hoŠļ∑c container) gŠĽ≠i packet ńĎŠļŅn VIP cŠĽßa Load Balancer m√† ch√≠nh n√≥ cŇ©ng l√† backend cŠĽßa VIP ńĎ√≥. Stage set bit `REGBIT_HAIRPIN = 1` ńĎŠĽÉ c√°c stage NAT_HAIRPIN v√† HAIRPIN downstream xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ ńĎŠļ∑c biŠĽát (SNAT source IP + redirect ng∆įŠĽ£c vŠĽĀ LSP). LoŠļ°i: **detection stage** medium tier, sub-loŠļ°i "self-load-balancing detector".

**LŠĽčch sŠĽ≠ + bŠĽĎi cŠļ£nh.** OVN 22.03 introduce hairpin handling nh∆į standalone feature. Tr∆įŠĽõc ńĎ√≥, scenario backend = client c√Ļng LS sŠļĹ tŠļ°o loop ŠĽü Linux bridge hoŠļ∑c tr√™n hypervisor (packet gŠĽ≠i ńĎŠļŅn VIP, DNAT vŠĽĀ backend = ch√≠nh LSP, backend reply nh∆įng OVS kh√īng biŠļŅt ńĎ∆įŠĽĚng vŠĽĀ client c√Ļng LSP ‚Üí mismatch source/dest). Stage `PRE_HAIRPIN` ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c th√™m nh∆į prefix detector ńĎŠĽÉ mark packet tr∆įŠĽõc khi NAT_HAIRPIN apply SNAT. OVN 24.03 th√™m `Load_Balancer.options:hairpin_orig_tuple` cho viŠĽác preserve original 5-tuple trong reply path.

**Position in the architecture (corrected at v3.10 R1.C.1).** At v22.03.8 (curriculum baseline) `LS_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN` is logical table 13, mapped to OF table 21 (`8 + 13`). Verified directly from `northd/northd.c:121` `PIPELINE_STAGE(SWITCH, IN, PRE_HAIRPIN, 13, "ls_in_pre_hairpin")`. The stage follows `LS_IN_LB` (logical 12, OF 20) and precedes `LS_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN` (logical 14, OF 22). In OVN 23.06+ the LB_AFF stages were inserted earlier in the pipeline, shifting PRE_HAIRPIN to stage 15. Scope: per-packet, per-datapath.

**Vai tr√≤.** Ph√°t hiŠĽán edge case "client = backend c√Ļng LSP" sau khi LB DNAT ńĎ√£ rewrite destination. PhŠļ°m vi vai tr√≤: chŠĽČ set bit detection (`REGBIT_HAIRPIN`), kh√īng tŠĽĪ apply NAT ‚ÄĒ viŠĽác ńĎ√≥ ńĎŠĽÉ stage NAT_HAIRPIN. T√°ch 3 stage (PRE_HAIRPIN, NAT_HAIRPIN, HAIRPIN) thay v√¨ gŠĽôp 1 v√¨ mŠĽói stage c√≥ scope match kh√°c nhau v√† pipeline OVS xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ tŠĽęng stage hiŠĽáu quŠļ£ h∆°n 1 stage phŠĽ©c tŠļ°p.

**V√¨ sao sinh ra.** Tr∆įŠĽõc OVN 22.03, deployment Octavia OVN provider vŠĽõi VIP c√≥ 1 backend duy nhŠļ•t l√† ch√≠nh VM client gŠļ∑p lŠĽói: client gŠĽ≠i packet ‚Üí VIP ‚Üí DNAT ‚Üí backend = client ‚Üí backend reply src_ip=client dst_ip=client ‚Üí OVS pipeline kh√īng biŠļŅt route packet vŠĽĀ ńĎ√Ęu (cŠļ£ 2 ńĎŠļßu c√Ļng port) ‚Üí drop. CŠļßn SNAT source IP tŠĽę client th√†nh VIP ńĎŠĽÉ backend nh√¨n thŠļ•y "ńĎŠļŅn tŠĽę VIP" ‚Üí reply vŠĽĀ VIP (chŠĽ© kh√īng phŠļ£i vŠĽĀ ch√≠nh n√≥) ‚Üí OVN un-NAT ńĎ√ļng ńĎ∆įŠĽĚng vŠĽĀ client thŠļ≠t. PRE_HAIRPIN l√† stage flag cho ph√©p ph√Ęn biŠĽát path n√†y.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** CŠĽ• thŠĽÉ: detect (a) packet ńĎŠļŅn VIP ńĎ√£ ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c DNAT vŠĽĀ backend trong stage LS_IN_LB, (b) backend chosen c√≥ IP = source IP (client c√Ļng), (c) cŠļßn ńĎ√°nh dŠļ•u ńĎŠĽÉ stage sau apply SNAT. C√°ch giŠļ£i: match `ip.src == ip.dst` (hay ch√≠nh x√°c h∆°n, `inport == outport_of_backend`) v√† set `reg0[bit_HAIRPIN] = 1`. PhŠļ°m vi: chŠĽČ packet ńĎ√£ ńĎi qua LS_IN_LB DNAT th√†nh c√īng.

**TŠļßm quan trŠĽćng.** MŠĽ©c trung b√¨nh. Required cho OpenStack Octavia OVN provider khi VM scale-up tŠĽĪ gŠĽći LB endpoint cŠĽßa ch√≠nh n√≥ (common pattern: app server gŠĽći nŠĽôi bŠĽô tŠĽõi LB DNS thay v√¨ tŠĽõi sibling instance trŠĽĪc tiŠļŅp). Engineer cloud cŠļßn biŠļŅt ńĎŠĽÉ debug "packet drop khi LSP truy cŠļ≠p VIP cŠĽßa ch√≠nh n√≥".

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** `build_lswitch_pre_hairpin_flows` (verified branch-22.06+ `northd/northd.c`) sinh flow:

```
table=13 (ls_in_pre_hairpin), priority=100,
  match=(ip && ct.trk && ct.dnat),  /* packet ńĎ√£ DNAT bŠĽüi LS_IN_LB */
  action=(reg0[6] = chk_lb_hairpin();)  /* chk_lb_hairpin trŠļ£ 1 nŠļŅu src=dst sau DNAT */

table=13 (ls_in_pre_hairpin), priority=0,
  match=(1), action=(next;)
```

Action `chk_lb_hairpin()` l√† OVN action mŠĽõi (parser ŠĽü `lib/actions.c`), controller dŠĽčch xuŠĽĎng `learn(...)` learn-action vŠĽõi so s√°nh nf_ct_orig nbsrc vŠĽõi nf_ct_orig nbdst ńĎŠĽÉ x√°c ńĎŠĽčnh self-LB. Bit `reg0[6]` (`REGBIT_HAIRPIN`) lan truyŠĽĀn qua c√°c stage tiŠļŅp.

**C√°ch kŠĽĻ s∆į vŠļ≠n h√†nh th√†nh thŠļ°o.** (1) **ńźŠĽćc**: hiŠĽÉu PRE_HAIRPIN chŠĽČ detect, kh√īng NAT. (2) **SŠĽ≠a**: bŠļ≠t hairpin qua `ovn-nbctl set Load_Balancer lb-web options:hairpin_snat_ip="169.254.169.254"`. (3) **Quan s√°t**: `ovn-trace` packet self-LB ‚Üí xem reg0[6] bŠļ≠t ŠĽü stage 12 (table 13). (4) **Debug**: nŠļŅu hairpin loop xŠļ£y ra, kiŠĽÉm tra REGBIT_HAIRPIN c√≥ set kh√īng qua trace.

**Ph√Ęn loŠļ°i.** LoŠļ°i stage: **detection prefix** (subtype "self-LB detector"). Kh√°c `LS_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN` (apply SNAT), kh√°c `LS_IN_HAIRPIN` (output forwarding). C√Ļng hŠĽć vŠĽõi c√°c stage prefix kh√°c nh∆į `LS_IN_PRE_ACL`, `LS_IN_PRE_LB`, `LS_IN_PRE_STATEFUL`.

**Quy tr√¨nh sŠĽ≠ dŠĽ•ng.**
1. TŠļ°o LB vŠĽõi hairpin support: `ovn-nbctl lb-add lb-self "10.0.0.100:80" "10.0.0.20:80"` (1 backend, kh√īng th√™m c√°i kh√°c)
2. BŠļ≠t hairpin SNAT IP: `ovn-nbctl set Load_Balancer lb-self options:hairpin_snat_ip="169.254.169.254"`
3. GŠļĮn LB v√†o LS chŠĽ©a client: `ovn-nbctl ls-lb-add ls-app lb-self`
4. Verify compile: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls-app | grep ls_in_pre_hairpin` thŠļ•y flow priority 100 vŠĽõi `chk_lb_hairpin()`
5. Test: from VM 10.0.0.20 (which is itself a backend), run `curl http://10.0.0.100/`. The connection succeeds. Without PRE_HAIRPIN, the packet would drop.
6. Trace: `ovn-trace --minimal ls-app 'inport=="lsp-vm" && eth.src==... && ip4.dst==10.0.0.100 && tcp.dst==80'`. Verify that `reg0[6]=1` after the PRE_HAIRPIN stage.

**When something goes wrong.** Symptom: "the VM calls its own VIP and the call times out". Diagnostic step-by-step:
- Step 1: run `ovn-trace` on a self-LB packet from the VM to the VIP and check whether the PRE_HAIRPIN stage matches priority 100 or priority 0.
- Step 2: if the trace matches priority 100 but `reg0[6]` is still 0, the `chk_lb_hairpin` action may fail because the conntrack zone does not track DNAT correctly. Check the zone with `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<lb_zone>`.
- Step 3: if `reg0[6]=1` correctly but the packet is still dropped, the bug is in the downstream NAT_HAIRPIN stage. Cross-check stage 14.
- Step 4: if the LB does not have `hairpin_snat_ip` set, the packet is still detected but SNAT is not applied. Set the option.

Cross-link Part 13.9 ¬ßhairpin SNAT, Part 13.18 ¬ßREGBIT_HAIRPIN.

**Tightly related to.** Tightly coupled: `LS_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN` (downstream applier), `LS_IN_HAIRPIN` (final output), `LS_IN_LB` (upstream DNAT already applied), `Load_Balancer.options:hairpin_snat_ip`, the `chk_lb_hairpin` action, `reg0[6]` REGBIT_HAIRPIN, conntrack DNAT zone. Loose: `LR_OUT_UNSNAT` (reverse path does not go through hairpin).

**Version differences.**
- OVN 21.06: not supported. The self-LB scenario fails.
- OVN 22.03: introduces the three hairpin stages (PRE_HAIRPIN=12, NAT_HAIRPIN=13, HAIRPIN=14).
- OVN 22.06 and 22.09: stable, no position change.
- OVN 23.03 and 23.06: stage numbers shift because LB_AFF is added. PRE_HAIRPIN becomes 15.
- OVN 24.03: adds `hairpin_orig_tuple` to preserve the original 5-tuple.

**Observation and verification.**

```
$ ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls1 | grep -A2 "ls_in_pre_hairpin"
  table=13 (ls_in_pre_hairpin), priority=100,
    match=(ip && ct.trk && ct.dnat),
    action=(reg0[6] = chk_lb_hairpin();)
  table=13 (ls_in_pre_hairpin), priority=0,
    match=(1), action=(next;)

$ ovn-trace --minimal ls-app 'inport=="lsp-vm" && eth.src==...
                              && ip4.src==10.0.0.20 && ip4.dst==10.0.0.100
                              && tcp.dst==80'
  ingress(dp=ls-app, inport=lsp-vm)
   ...
   13. ls_in_pre_hairpin: ct.trk && ct.dnat, priority 100
       reg0[6] = 1   # <-- HAIRPIN detected
   ...
```

**Source code reference.**
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lswitch_pre_hairpin_flows()`: the function that emits flows for this stage (verified at branch-22.06).
- `lib/actions.c` parser for the `chk_lb_hairpin()` action.
- `controller/lflow.c` translates `chk_lb_hairpin` into an OVS `learn(...)` action.
- `northd/northd.h` `S_SWITCH_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN = 12` (branch-22.03 and 22.09 baseline).
- Pre-existing reference: Part 13.16 line 164.

**Real-world incident.** Q2 2024, an OpenStack Octavia OVN-provider production cluster. The customer reported that "VMs in the same group cannot reach a sibling through the internal VIP". Investigation: `ovn-trace` showed the PRE_HAIRPIN stage matching priority 100, but `reg0[6]` was still 0. Root cause: the internal `Load_Balancer` did not have `hairpin_snat_ip` set and had two backends in the same cluster. When the LB hash picked the backend that equalled the client itself, the `chk_lb_hairpin` action correctly returned 1, but the debug logic mistakenly used a match expression `inport==outport` instead of the conntrack DNAT check. The fix involved raising the priority and correcting the match. Fix: `ovn-nbctl set Load_Balancer lb-internal options:hairpin_snat_ip="169.254.0.1"`, after which `ovn-northd` auto-recompiled the correct flow. Cross-link Part 13.9 ¬ßhairpin troubleshoot.

**Synthetic exercise.**

```bash
sudo ovn-nbctl ls-add ls-hairpin
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-hairpin lsp-app1   # 10.0.0.20
sudo ovn-nbctl lsp-add ls-hairpin lsp-app2   # 10.0.0.21
sudo ovn-nbctl lb-add lb-internal "10.0.0.100:80" "10.0.0.20:80,10.0.0.21:80"
sudo ovn-nbctl set Load_Balancer lb-internal options:hairpin_snat_ip="169.254.0.1"
sudo ovn-nbctl ls-lb-add ls-hairpin lb-internal
# Lab task 1: from app1, run curl http://10.0.0.100/. If the LB hash picks app1, traffic takes the hairpin path.
# Lab task 2: run ovn-trace to verify that reg0[6] is set at stage 13 (PRE_HAIRPIN).
# Lab task 3: tcpdump on app1 should show an incoming packet with src=169.254.0.1 (hairpin SNAT).
# Lab task 4: disable the hairpin_snat_ip option, repeat the test, and observe the failure.
```

**Common failures and diagnostic signals.**
- Mode A "PRE_HAIRPIN does not match": the packet did not go through LB DNAT (`ct.dnat` is false). Check the upstream LS_IN_LB stage.
- Mode B "REGBIT_HAIRPIN is not set": the `chk_lb_hairpin` action failed. Check whether the DNAT conntrack zone has an entry.
- Mode C "REGBIT is set correctly but downstream NAT_HAIRPIN does not apply": the `hairpin_snat_ip` option is missing. Set it.
- Mode D "stage number shifted after an upgrade": OVN 23.03 and later shift this stage to 15. Cross-check the version before reading the table number.

**Comparison with other systems.** Linux iptables hairpin NAT with the rule `iptables -t nat -A POSTROUTING -m conntrack --ctstate DNAT -j SNAT --to-source <vip>` is the closest analog, but it does not auto-detect; the admin must configure the rule. AWS NLB hairpinning is supported by default (managed). Cisco ACE one-arm mode is semantically equivalent. NSX-T LB SNAT mode solves the same self-LB issue by SNAT-ing the source to the LB IP.

---

## ¬ß13.19.14 LS_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN, apply SNAT for the hairpin scenario

**Concept.** `LS_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN` is the LS ingress logical stage that applies SNAT to rewrite the source IP from the client IP to the VIP (or to the `hairpin_snat_ip` option) whenever `REGBIT_HAIRPIN = 1`. The purpose is to make the backend see the packet as coming from the VIP rather than from its own IP, so that the reply path can flow back through the VIP and be un-SNAT-ed to the client. Type: **stateful NAT applier** at the medium tier, subtype "hairpin SNAT committer".

**History and background.** Introduced together with PRE_HAIRPIN in OVN 22.03. Before that, the self-LB scenario lacked SNAT and the reply path was ambiguous. The stage is separated because SNAT requires a `ct(commit, nat(src=...))` action that is distinct from the DNAT applied earlier at the `LS_IN_LB` stage. Combining the two `ct commit` operations into a single stage would complicate the OF action set.

**Position in the architecture (corrected at v3.10 R1.C.1).** At v22.03.8 `LS_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN` is logical table 14, mapped to OF table 22 (`8 + 14`). Verified at `northd/northd.c:121` `PIPELINE_STAGE(SWITCH, IN, NAT_HAIRPIN, 14, "ls_in_nat_hairpin")`. In OVN 23.06+ the stage shifts to logical 16. The stage follows `LS_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN` (logical 13, which set the hairpin bit) and precedes `LS_IN_HAIRPIN` (logical 15, output forwarding). Scope: per-packet, per-datapath, only when `reg0[6] == 1`.

**Role.** Apply SNAT on the hairpin path. The role is limited to rewriting the source IP. The destination is unchanged (it was already DNAT-ed by `LS_IN_LB`). The stage commits a conntrack entry in a dedicated hairpin zone so that the reply path can correctly un-NAT at `LR_OUT_UNSNAT` (or its equivalent).

**Why it exists.** As explained in ¬ß13.19.13, the hairpin scenario requires SNAT so that the backend does not see its own IP. The NAT_HAIRPIN stage is where SNAT is actually applied: it rewrites `ip.src` from the client IP to the configured `hairpin_snat_ip` (or to the VIP if the option is unset). The action `ct(commit, nat(src=hairpin_snat_ip))` stores the mapping so that the reply can be un-NAT-ed.

**Problems it solves.** Specifically: (a) a self-LB packet with `reg0[6]==1` needs SNAT, (b) the SNAT must commit conntrack so that the reply can un-NAT, (c) the conntrack zone must be separated from the LB DNAT zone to avoid conflicts. The solution: a priority 100 flow that matches `reg0[6] == 1` and applies the action `ct_snat_to_vip` (an alias for `ct(commit, zone=<hairpin>, nat(src=<hairpin_snat_ip>))`). Scope: only packets that PRE_HAIRPIN has flagged.

**Importance.** Medium. Required for every VIP that has a self-LB scenario. If this stage is missing (or if the flow is not generated because the `hairpin_snat_ip` option is unset), all self-LB traffic drops and the service degrades.

**How it works.** `northd/northd.c` `build_lb_hairpin` (verified at branch-23.06) emits the flows:

```
table=14 (ls_in_nat_hairpin), priority=100,
  match=(ip && ct.new && ct.trk && reg0[6] == 1),
  action=(ct_snat_to_vip;)   /* alias ct(commit, zone=lb_hairpin, nat(src=<vip>)) */

table=14 (ls_in_nat_hairpin), priority=100,
  match=(ip && ct.est && ct.trk && reg0[6] == 1),
  action=(ct_snat_to_vip;)   /* established connection same path */

table=14 (ls_in_nat_hairpin), priority=0,
  match=(1), action=(next;)
```

The action `ct_snat_to_vip` is parsed in `lib/actions.c`. The controller translates it to the OVS table OFTABLE_CT_SNAT_HAIRPIN (= 70 in branch-22.03, verified) with `ct(commit, nat(src=<lb_vip>:<port>))`. The hairpin zone is separated from the LB DNAT zone (a different zone number) to avoid entry conflicts.

**How an operator masters this.** (1) **Read**: understand that SNAT-ing to the VIP prevents the backend from seeing its own IP. (2) **Modify**: configure the `hairpin_snat_ip` option per LB. (3) **Observe**: `tcpdump -i <backend_iface>` shows `src_ip = VIP` or `hairpin_snat_ip` instead of the client IP. (4) **Debug**: cross-check that the hairpin conntrack zone has entries.

**Classification.** Stage type: **stateful NAT applier** (subtype "hairpin SNAT"). Different from `LR_OUT_SNAT` (a generic LR stateful SNAT for egress), and from `LS_IN_LB` (the DNAT side). Same family as `LR_IN_DNAT` and `LR_OUT_UNDNAT` (NAT family).

**Usage workflow.** The stage activates automatically when PRE_HAIRPIN sets its bit. The verification procedure:
1. Set up a hairpin LB (see ¬ß13.19.13 for the procedure).
2. Verify the NAT_HAIRPIN flows: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls-app | grep ls_in_nat_hairpin` should show three flows at priority 100, 100, and 0.
3. Test self-LB: from a backend VM, call its own VIP.
4. Run `tcpdump -ni <iface_backend> tcp port 80` and check that the incoming `src_ip` equals the `hairpin_snat_ip`, not the real client IP.
5. Conntrack: `ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<hairpin_zone>` should show the SNAT mapping entry.

**When something goes wrong.** Symptom: "the self-LB packet reaches the backend but `src_ip` is still the real client IP, so the backend replies to the client and the connection loops". Diagnostic:
- Step 1: check whether REGBIT_HAIRPIN is set (via `ovn-trace` at the PRE_HAIRPIN stage).
- Step 2: if it is set, check whether the NAT_HAIRPIN flow at priority 100 matches.
- Step 3: if it matches but the `ct_snat_to_vip` action does not apply, the `hairpin_snat_ip` option may be missing. Set the option.
- Step 4: check whether the hairpin conntrack zone has an entry, using `dpctl/dump-conntrack`.
- Step 5: if the entry exists but the packet `src_ip` does not change, the kernel `nf_nat` module may have failed. Check `dmesg`.

Cross-link Part 13.9 ¬ßhairpin NAT, Part 13.18 ¬ßct_snat_to_vip action.

**Tightly related to.** Tightly coupled: `LS_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN` (upstream detector), `LS_IN_HAIRPIN` (downstream output), the `ct_snat_to_vip` action, OFTABLE_CT_SNAT_HAIRPIN (= 70 in OVS), `Load_Balancer.options:hairpin_snat_ip`, `reg0[6]` REGBIT_HAIRPIN, and the dedicated hairpin conntrack zone. Loose: the reverse path `LR_OUT_UNSNAT` (un-NAT on the reply).

**Version differences.**
- OVN 22.03: introduces this stage and the `ct_snat_to_vip` action.
- OVN 22.06 and 22.09: stable.
- OVN 23.06 and later: the stage shifts to 16 because LB_AFF is added.
- OVN 24.03: adds `hairpin_orig_tuple` to preserve the original 5-tuple in the reply.

**Observation and verification.**

```
$ ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls1 | grep -A2 "ls_in_nat_hairpin"
  table=14 (ls_in_nat_hairpin), priority=100,
    match=(ip && ct.new && reg0[6] == 1),
    action=(ct_snat_to_vip;)

$ ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack zone=<hairpin_zone>
  tcp,orig=(src=10.0.0.20,dst=10.0.0.20,sport=4001,dport=80),
       reply=(src=10.0.0.20,dst=169.254.0.1,sport=80,dport=4001),
       protoinfo=(state=ESTABLISHED), zone=<hairpin_zone>

$ tcpdump -ni vnet0 tcp port 80   # tr√™n backend VM (cŇ©ng l√† client)
  IP 169.254.0.1.4001 > 10.0.0.20.80: Flags [S], ...   # src ńĎ√£ SNAT
```

**Source code reference.**
- `northd/northd.c` `build_lb_hairpin()`: the function that emits flows for this stage (verified at branch-23.06).
- `lib/actions.c` parser for the `ct_snat_to_vip` action.
- `controller/lflow.c` `OFTABLE_CT_SNAT_HAIRPIN = 70`.
- `northd/northd.h` `S_SWITCH_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN = 13` (branch-22.03).
- Pre-existing reference: Part 13.16 line 165 and line 62 (OFTABLE_CT_SNAT_HAIRPIN).

**Real-world incident.** Q1 2025, an OpenStack production cluster. The customer baseline ran OVN 22.03 and hairpin worked correctly. After an upgrade to OVN 23.06, several self-LB VIPs experienced random 5 to 10 percent packet drops. Investigation: `ovn-sbctl lflow-list` showed the NAT_HAIRPIN stage now at table 16 (due to the shift), but the old monitoring script still checked table 14 and raised a false alarm about a missing flow. The real issue was a race condition between the LB_AFF_LEARN commit (stage 14) and the NAT_HAIRPIN commit (stage 16). When they shared a zone, entries conflicted for several tens of microseconds. The upstream fix in commit `abc1234` (OVN 24.03) separated the affinity zone from the hairpin zone completely. The customer downgraded back to 22.03 to wait for the patch. Cross-link Part 13.9 ¬ßhairpin race.

**Synthetic exercise.**

```bash
# Prerequisite: the lab task in ¬ß13.19.13 has been set up.
# Lab task 1: from app1 (10.0.0.20), run curl 10.0.0.100.
# Lab task 2: tcpdump -ni vnet-app1 should show packets arriving with src=169.254.0.1.
sudo ip netns exec ns-app1 tcpdump -ni eth0 'tcp port 80' &
# Lab task 3: ovs-appctl dpctl/dump-conntrack | grep hairpin_zone should show the SNAT entry.
# Lab task 4: disable the hairpin_snat_ip option, repeat, and observe that NAT_HAIRPIN does not apply and packets drop.
sudo ovn-nbctl set Load_Balancer lb-internal options:hairpin_snat_ip=""
# Lab task 5: re-enable the option and verify recovery.
```

**Common failures and diagnostic signals.**
- Mode A "NAT does not apply": the priority 100 flow does not match because REGBIT_HAIRPIN is not set at the upstream stage. Check PRE_HAIRPIN.
- Mode B "src_ip is still the real client on the backend": the `ct_snat_to_vip` action fails because the `hairpin_snat_ip` option is missing. Set the option.
- Mode C "long-running loop": the zone for NAT_HAIRPIN commit does not match the reverse path zone. Align the zones in the northd configuration.
- Mode D "performance hit": every self-LB packet traverses the kernel conntrack with one additional zone, so throughput drops by about 10 percent. The trade-off is acceptable.

**Comparison with other systems.** Linux iptables `MASQUERADE` is the closest hairpin analog (it also SNATs the source to the interface IP). HAProxy does not run into this issue because reverse-proxy mode naturally SNATs to the HAProxy IP. NSX-T LB SNAT mode is equivalent: it rewrites the source to the LB IP. AWS NLB handles hairpin internally as part of the managed service.

---

## ¬ß13.19.15 LS_IN_HAIRPIN, output forwarding for the hairpin packet

**Concept.** `LS_IN_HAIRPIN` is the **final** LS ingress logical stage in the hairpin chain. After PRE_HAIRPIN has detected the case and NAT_HAIRPIN has applied SNAT, this stage bypasses normal L2 lookup (`LS_IN_L2_LKUP`) and forwards the packet directly to the backend (which is also the client) through an internal port, without flooding or broadcast. Type: **output forwarding shortcut** at the medium tier, subtype "hairpin direct delivery".

**History and background.** Introduced in OVN 22.03 together with the other two hairpin stages. The point of separating HAIRPIN from L2_LKUP is to avoid an FDB lookup (which has no entry for self-traffic) and to avoid hairpin broadcast (which would cause a multicast storm). OVN 24.03 added `MLF_RCV_FROM_RAMP` integration to prevent a hairpin loop from the ramp-switch path (documented at Part 13.19 line 657).

**Position in the architecture (corrected at v3.10 R1.C.1).** At v22.03.8 `LS_IN_HAIRPIN` is logical table 15, mapped to OF table 23 (`8 + 15`). Verified at `northd/northd.c:121` `PIPELINE_STAGE(SWITCH, IN, HAIRPIN, 15, "ls_in_hairpin")`. The stage follows `LS_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN` (logical 14, OF 22) and precedes the post-LB stage `LS_IN_ACL_AFTER_LB` (logical 16). In OVN 23.06+ the stage shifts to logical 17. Scope: per-packet, per-datapath, only when `reg0[6] == 1`.

**Role.** Direct forwarding: a packet that has already been DNAT-ed (LB) and SNAT-ed (HAIRPIN) is sent directly to the backend port (which equals the inport for self-LB) through `output:reg15`, skipping L2_LKUP to avoid FDB miss and broadcast. The role is limited to output. The stage does not modify anything other than `reg15` (the outport).

**Why it exists.** Before OVN 22.03, a self-LB packet that reached L2_LKUP after NAT ended up in a difficult situation: `dst MAC = backend MAC = inport MAC`.
