## ¬ß13.19.39 LS_IN_STATEFUL ‚ÄĒ commit conntrack entry cho new connection

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LS_IN_STATEFUL` l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 17** trong LS ingress, OF table 25 tr√™n br-int (theo 13.16 d√≤ng 168). Stage l√† **ńĎiŠĽÉm cuŠĽĎi stateful** cŠĽßa ingress LS pipeline: khi `REGBIT_CONNTRACK_COMMIT=reg0[1]` ńĎ√£ ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c set bŠĽüi `LS_IN_ACL` (allow-related) hoŠļ∑c `LS_IN_LB` (DNAT commit), stage n√†y emit `ct(commit, zone=reg13, exec(...))` ńĎŠĽÉ ghi connection v√†o kernel conntrack table ‚Üí reply path tŠĽĪ ńĎŠĽông ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c ph√©p qua. LoŠļ°i: **pipeline stateful committer peripheral**, sub-loŠļ°i "conntrack final commit".

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage 17 (OF table 25). ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LS_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN/HAIRPIN/NAT_HAIRPIN` (stage 13-16) v√† tr∆įŠĽõc `LS_IN_ARP_ND_RSP` (stage 18). Scope: per-packet tr√™n LS c√≥ ACL stateful (`allow-related`) hoŠļ∑c LB.

**Vai tr√≤ + v√¨ sao sinh ra.** OVN ACL `allow-related` cŠļßn commit connection ńĎŠĽÉ reply path (kh√īng match rule allow r√Ķ r√†ng v√¨ rule chŠĽČ allow forward direction) ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c tŠĽĪ ńĎŠĽông cho qua qua match `ct.est && !ct.rpl`. Stage n√†y t√°ch commit ra khŠĽŹi `LS_IN_ACL` ńĎŠĽÉ ńĎŠļ£m bŠļ£o commit chŠĽČ xŠļ£y ra **sau** mŠĽći quyŠļŅt ńĎŠĽčnh stateful kh√°c (LB DNAT, hairpin SNAT) ho√†n tŠļ•t, tr√°nh commit sai 5-tuple. T√°ch stage cŇ©ng cho ph√©p `ct_label.blocked` flag ghi ńĎŠĽďng thŠĽĚi vŠĽõi commit (encode policy denied state v√†o label cho stage downstream tham chiŠļŅu).

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** (a) Single commit point thay v√¨ rŠļ£i r√°c nhiŠĽĀu stage, (b) commit sau khi DNAT/SNAT ńĎ√£ apply (5-tuple ńĎ√ļng vŠĽõi connection ngo√†i), (c) commit k√®m `ct_label` mark policy decision, (d) skip nŠļŅu REGBIT_CONNTRACK_COMMIT kh√īng set (stateless flow).

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** H√†m sinh flow: `build_stateful` trong `northd/northd.c` (verified branch-22.03 stage token `S_SWITCH_IN_STATEFUL`). Function sinh 2 nh√≥m flow ch√≠nh: nh√≥m commit cho ACL allow-related, nh√≥m commit cho LB DNAT:

```
table=25 (ls_in_stateful), priority=100,
  match=(reg0[1] == 1),                              # REGBIT_CONNTRACK_COMMIT
  action=(ct_commit { ct_label.blocked = 0; }; next;)
table=25, priority=100,
  match=(reg0[2] == 1),                              # REGBIT_CONNTRACK_NAT
  action=(ct_lb_mark;)
table=25, priority=0, match=(1), action=(next;)
```

Action `ct_commit { ct_label.blocked = 0; }` l√† syntax OVN expand th√†nh `ct(commit, zone=NXM_NX_REG13[0..15], exec(set_field:0/0x1->ct_label))` trong OF rule. `ct_lb_mark` commit DNAT mapping v√†o conntrack zone LB (separate tŠĽę zone ACL).

**Quy tr√¨nh + c√°ch quan s√°t.** TŠļ°o LS vŠĽõi ACL `allow-related` + LB. Send connection mŠĽõi ‚Üí ovn-trace b√°o stage 17 emit `ct_commit`. `conntrack -L -z <zone_id>` (Linux conntrack tool) verify entry vŠĽęa tŠļ°o. `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=25` xem rule + n_packets.

**Kh√°c biŠĽát phi√™n bŠļ£n.** OVN 2.6 (2017) introduce stage stateful ńĎ∆°n giŠļ£n. OVN 2.7 th√™m `ct_label.blocked` cho ACL kill connection mid-flow. OVN 21.06 th√™m `ct_lb_mark` action thay `ct_lb` cŇ©. OVN 22.03 baseline ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh. OVN 24.03 tŠĽĎi ∆įu compile khi LS c√≥ > 1000 LB endpoint.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** `REGBIT_CONNTRACK_COMMIT=reg0[1]`, `REGBIT_CONNTRACK_NAT=reg0[2]`, `ct_label.blocked` bit, `reg13` (ct_zone), action `ct_commit` + `ct_lb_mark`, `LS_IN_ACL` (upstream set REGBIT cho allow-related), `LS_IN_LB` (upstream set REGBIT cho DNAT), `LS_OUT_STATEFUL` (egress sibling). Xem PhŠļßn 13.18 (REGBIT catalog), PhŠļßn 9.24 (OVS conntrack), PhŠļßn 4.8 (ct_label).

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.** H√†m `build_stateful` trong `northd/northd.c` branch-22.03; stage token `S_SWITCH_IN_STATEFUL` table 17 logical, table 25 OF. Action `ct_commit` parser: `lib/actions.c` `parse_CT_COMMIT_V2`. Conntrack runtime: `lib/conntrack.c` (OVS kernel + userspace).

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Linux iptables `-m conntrack --ctstate NEW -j ACCEPT` + implicit kernel commit analog; iptables kh√īng t√°ch commit th√†nh stage ri√™ng, kernel tŠĽĪ commit khi packet pass cuŠĽĎi chain. Cisco ASA stateful inspection commit implicit. OVN kh√°c biŠĽát: explicit commit stage cho ph√©p policy fine-grained (chŠĽćn commit hay kh√īng, ńĎ√≠nh label), t√°ch zone ACL kh√°c zone LB cho hairpin support.

## ¬ß13.19.40 LS_IN_DNS_LOOKUP ‚ÄĒ phŠļ£n hŠĽďi DNS query native trong pipeline

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LS_IN_DNS_LOOKUP` l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 21** trong LS ingress, OF table 29 tr√™n br-int (theo 13.16 d√≤ng 172). Stage match DNS query packet (UDP dst port 53), gŠĽći action `dns_lookup()` ńĎŠĽÉ tra cŠĽ©u fqdn trong NBDB `DNS_Records` map (map `fqdn ‚Üí IP`); nŠļŅu hit, action build DNS response payload trong packet hiŠĽán tŠļ°i + set `REGBIT_DNS_LOOKUP_RESULT=reg0[4]=1` ńĎŠĽÉ stage downstream emit reply. LoŠļ°i: **pipeline DNS server inline peripheral**, sub-loŠļ°i "DNS query interceptor".

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage 21 (OF table 29). ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LS_IN_DHCP_RESPONSE` (stage 20) v√† tr∆įŠĽõc `LS_IN_EXTERNAL_PORT` (stage 22 hoŠļ∑c t∆į∆°ng ńĎ∆į∆°ng). Scope: per-packet (chŠĽČ DNS UDP port 53), per-LS c√≥ `Logical_Switch.dns_records` config.

**Vai tr√≤ + v√¨ sao sinh ra.** Tenant trong cloud cŠļßn DNS resolution cho service discovery (`db.tenant1.local ‚Üí 10.0.0.10`) m√† kh√īng phŠļ£i triŠĽÉn khai dnsmasq external + kh√īng phŠļ£i ńĎŠļ©y DNS query l√™n upstream. OVN intercept DNS query native trong pipeline ‚Üí giŠļ£m latency tŠĽę ms (network round-trip ńĎŠļŅn dnsmasq) xuŠĽĎng ¬Ķs (in-kernel datapath response). Tr∆įŠĽõc c√≥ DNS native, tenant phŠļ£i config dnsmasq tr√™n hypervisor manual.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** (a) Native DNS resolution kh√īng cŠļßn daemon external, (b) declarative qua NBDB `DNS_Records`, (c) per-LS scope (mŠĽói tenant c√≥ records ri√™ng), (d) latency thŠļ•p v√¨ xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ in-kernel/userspace OVS trŠĽĪc tiŠļŅp, (e) fallback transparent (nŠļŅu fqdn kh√īng match local records, packet pass through ńĎŠļŅn upstream DNS).

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** H√†m sinh flow: `build_lswitch_dns_lookup_and_response` trong `northd/northd.c` (verified branch-22.03 stage token `S_SWITCH_IN_DNS_LOOKUP`, h√†m c√Ļng hŠĽć vŠĽõi DHCP_OPTIONS/RESPONSE pattern). Function sinh 2 nh√°nh:

```
table=29 (ls_in_dns_lookup), priority=100,
  match=(udp.dst == 53),
  action=(reg0[4] = dns_lookup(); next;)
table=29, priority=0, match=(1), action=(next;)
```

Action `dns_lookup` l√† **controller action**: packet upcall l√™n ovn-controller `pinctrl_handle_dns_lookup()` (`controller/pinctrl.c`), handler parse DNS query qname, lookup trong cache `DNS_Records` synced tŠĽę SBDB, nŠļŅu hit th√¨ build DNS response payload (RR section) ghi ńĎ√® v√†o packet payload + return REGBIT=1; nŠļŅu miss return REGBIT=0 (packet pass through). Stage tiŠļŅp `LS_IN_DNS_RESPONSE` (stage 22, kh√īng trong scope keyword n√†y) check REGBIT v√† emit reply.

**Quy tr√¨nh + c√°ch quan s√°t.** `ovn-nbctl set Logical_Switch ls1 dns_records=@dns1 -- --id=@dns1 create DNS records='{"web.local"="10.0.0.5"}'` provision DNS row. `ovn-sbctl lflow-list ls1 | grep ls_in_dns_lookup` xem flow. VM trong LS gŠĽ≠i `dig @<DNS server VIP> web.local` ‚Üí reply vŠĽĀ < 1ms. `tail -f /var/log/ovn/ovn-controller.log | grep dns_lookup` xem upcall handler trace.

**Kh√°c biŠĽát phi√™n bŠļ£n.** OVN 2.8 (2018) introduce DNS native vŠĽõi cŠļ∑p DNS_LOOKUP + DNS_RESPONSE. OVN 20.06 th√™m support reverse DNS (PTR record). OVN 22.03 baseline ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh. OVN 23.06 hŠĽó trŠĽ£ `DNS.options:server_response_max_size` cho large records. OVN 24.09 cŠļ£i thiŠĽán cache invalidation khi DNS_Records row update.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** NBDB `DNS` table (column `records` map fqdn‚ÜíIP, `external_ids`), `Logical_Switch.dns_records`, action `dns_lookup`, `REGBIT_DNS_LOOKUP_RESULT=reg0[4]`, `LS_IN_DNS_RESPONSE` (stage 22 sibling, emit reply), `controller/pinctrl.c` `pinctrl_handle_dns_lookup`. Xem PhŠļßn 13.10 (OVN DHCP+DNS native deep dive), PhŠļßn 13.18 (REGBIT catalog), PhŠļßn 4.9 (controller action). Loose: dnsmasq (alternative external daemon), external upstream DNS (passthrough fallback).

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.** H√†m `build_lswitch_dns_lookup_and_response` trong `northd/northd.c` branch-22.03 (sinh flow cho cŠļ£ DNS_LOOKUP + DNS_RESPONSE); stage token `S_SWITCH_IN_DNS_LOOKUP` table 21 logical, table 29 OF. Action parser: `lib/actions.c` `parse_DNS_LOOKUP`. Runtime handler: `controller/pinctrl.c` `pinctrl_handle_dns_lookup` parse DNS query/build response. NBDB schema: `ovn-nb.ovsschema` table `DNS`. Documented `ovn-northd.8.xml` mŠĽ•c "Ingress Table 21: DNS Lookup".

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** dnsmasq daemon analog (userspace, per-host). CoreDNS in K8s analog (cluster-wide pod). AWS Route 53 Resolver analog (managed). OVN kh√°c biŠĽát: DNS resolution xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ trŠĽĪc tiŠļŅp trong OVN pipeline qua controller upcall, kh√īng cŠļßn daemon ri√™ng; declarative qua NBDB DNS row + per-LS scope; cluster-wide visible qua SBDB; latency cŠĽĪc thŠļ•p v√¨ handler chŠļ°y trong ovn-controller process.

## ¬ß13.19.41 LR_IN_ARP_RESOLVE ‚ÄĒ gŠļĮn next-hop MAC cho packet sŠļĮp rŠĽĚi LR

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LR_IN_ARP_RESOLVE` l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 15** cŠĽßa LR ingress, OF table 23 tr√™n br-int (theo 13.16 d√≤ng 231). Stage l√† **ńĎiŠĽÉm cuŠĽĎi resolve** cŠĽßa chuŠĽói neighbor handling: sau khi `LR_IN_LOOKUP_NEIGHBOR` (stage 1) ńĎ√£ set `MFF_LOG_LOOKUP_NEIGHBOR=reg9[2]` b√°o cache hit/miss v√† `LR_IN_IP_ROUTING` (stage 11) ńĎ√£ ńĎŠļ∑t `xxreg0=<next-hop IP>` + `outport=<LRP egress>`, stage 23 n√†y c√≥ nhiŠĽám vŠĽ• ńĎŠļ∑t `eth.dst = <MAC of next-hop>` tŠĽę MAC_Binding cache (hoŠļ∑c tŠĽę Static_MAC_Binding). Khi cache c√≥ entry, set MAC trŠĽĪc tiŠļŅp + `next;`; khi miss, ńĎŠĽÉ `eth.dst` ch∆įa rewrite v√† defer `LR_IN_ARP_REQUEST` (stage 19) xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ emit ARP. LoŠļ°i: **pipeline ingress neighbor binding applier peripheral**, sub-loŠļ°i "MAC_Binding apply step".

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage logic 15, OF table 23. ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LR_IN_POLICY_ECMP` (stage 14, table 22) v√† tr∆įŠĽõc `LR_IN_CHK_PKT_LEN` (stage 16, table 24). Scope: per-packet, per-LR datapath, mŠĽći packet ńĎ√£ c√≥ routing decision ńĎŠĽĀu phŠļ£i ńĎi qua. C√Ļng bŠĽô ba stage neighbor: 1 (LOOKUP) ‚Üí 2 (LEARN) ‚Üí 15 (RESOLVE) ‚Üí 19 (REQUEST). T√°ch 4 stage n√†y cho ph√©p idempotent + ch√®n policy giŠĽĮa.

**Vai tr√≤ + v√¨ sao sinh ra.** MŠĽói packet egress qua LR cŠļßn `eth.dst` ńĎ√ļng = MAC cŠĽßa next-hop (LSP cŠĽßa subnet next-hop hoŠļ∑c external gateway MAC). NŠļŅu ńĎŠĽÉ chung trong IP_ROUTING, mŠĽći route entry phŠļ£i mang theo MAC, g√Ęy bloat. T√°ch RESOLVE ra: routing chŠĽČ cŠļßn biŠļŅt next-hop IP + outport, MAC binding lookup ri√™ng ‚Üí khi MAC_Binding cŠļ≠p nhŠļ≠t (gateway failover, ARP refresh) chŠĽČ cŠļßn update SBDB row, lflow IP_ROUTING kh√īng phŠļ£i recompile.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** (a) Decouple FIB tŠĽę MAC binding (FIB stable, MAC binding volatile), (b) cho ph√©p Static_MAC_Binding override dynamic learning, (c) gom ńĎiŠĽÉm "rewrite eth.dst" vŠĽĀ mŠĽôt stage ńĎŠĽÉ cookie debugging dŠĽÖ, (d) khi miss, REGBIT ńĎŠĽÉ stage 19 quyŠļŅt ńĎŠĽčnh emit ARP request, kh√īng emit lŠļ°i nŠļŅu vŠĽęa emit (rate-limit cŠļ•p pinctrl).

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** H√†m sinh flow: `build_lrouter_arp_resolve_flows` trong `northd/northd.c` branch-22.03 (token `S_ROUTER_IN_ARP_RESOLVE`). Function sinh 3 nh√≥m flow: (a) priority 100 match `outport == "lrp1" && reg0 == 10.0.0.10` (next-hop IP ńĎ√£ biŠļŅt) ‚Üí `eth.dst = aa:bb:cc:00:00:10; next;`; (b) priority 50 match `outport == "lrp1" && eth.dst == 00:00:00:00:00:00` (MAC ch∆įa set) ‚Üí `get_arp(outport, reg0); next;` (controller action lookup cache); (c) priority 0 catch-all `next;`. V√≠ dŠĽ• thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ:

```
table=23 (lr_in_arp_resolve), priority=100,
  match=(outport == "lrp-uplink" && reg0 == 10.0.0.254),
  action=(eth.dst = aa:bb:cc:dd:ee:01; next;)
table=23, priority=50,
  match=(ip4 && outport == "lrp-uplink"),
  action=(get_arp(outport, reg0); next;)
table=23, priority=0, match=(1), action=(next;)
```

Action `get_arp` upcall `pinctrl_handle_get_arp` ńĎŠĽÉ tra MAC_Binding runtime; nŠļŅu t√¨m thŠļ•y, controller install flow priority 100 mŠĽõi cho IP ńĎ√≥ (lazy population).

**Quy tr√¨nh + c√°ch quan s√°t.** `ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr-main | grep lr_in_arp_resolve` xem flow cho LR. `ovn-trace lr-main 'inport=="lrp1" && ip4.src==10.0.0.5 && ip4.dst==192.168.1.5'` thŠļ•y stage 23 set eth.dst. `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=23 | grep n_packets` xem traffic count. Khi gateway MAC thay ńĎŠĽēi (vRouter swap), monitor SBDB MAC_Binding row update + lflow recompile latency.

**Kh√°c biŠĽát phi√™n bŠļ£n.** OVN < 21.03: stage l√†m cŠļ£ lookup + resolve trong 1 stage (gŠĽôp). OVN 21.03 t√°ch LOOKUP + LEARN ra tr∆įŠĽõc, ARP_RESOLVE c√≤n nhiŠĽám vŠĽ• apply MAC. OVN 22.03 baseline ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh. OVN 23.06 cŠļ£i thiŠĽán priority 50 catch-all ńĎŠĽÉ kh√īng match packet ńĎ√£ ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c Static_MAC_Binding pre-populate. OVN 24.03 th√™m support multi-MAC binding cho ECMP next-hop kh√°c nhau.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** `MAC_Binding` table SBDB (input data), `Static_MAC_Binding` NBDB (config-driven), `xxreg0` next-hop IP register sau routing, `eth.dst` field rewrite, `LR_IN_LOOKUP_NEIGHBOR` (stage 1, set REGBIT), `LR_IN_LEARN_NEIGHBOR` (stage 2, insert MAC_Binding), `LR_IN_ARP_REQUEST` (stage 19, emit ARP nŠļŅu miss), `LR_OUT_DELIVERY` (consumer downstream cŠļßn eth.dst ńĎ√ļng). Xem 13.5 ¬ß13.5.1c.3 (MAC_Binding deep dive), 13.18 (REGBIT catalog), 13.16 d√≤ng 231.

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.** `northd/northd.c` h√†m `build_lrouter_arp_resolve_flows` xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ stage `S_ROUTER_IN_ARP_RESOLVE` table 15 logical, table 23 OF. Action `get_arp` parser `lib/actions.c` `parse_GET_ARP`. Runtime handler `controller/pinctrl.c` `pinctrl_handle_get_arp_or_nd`. SBDB schema `MAC_Binding` table.

**SŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ + lŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p.** Symptom: traffic egress LR drop sau gateway failover. Cause: MAC_Binding cache stale (cŇ© MAC gateway chassis active, gateway mŠĽõi ch∆įa ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c hŠĽćc). Diagnose: `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=23 | grep <gateway_ip>` thŠļ•y MAC cŇ© ‚Üí `ovn-sbctl destroy MAC_Binding <uuid>` clean; pre-populate Static_MAC_Binding. Common pitfall: route point ńĎŠļŅn next-hop ngo√†i subnet LRP ‚Üí ARP lookup fail m√£i ‚Üí mŠĽći packet stuck ŠĽü priority 50.

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Linux kernel rewrite L2 dst qua `neigh` stack analog. Cisco IOS ARP cache lookup tr∆įŠĽõc transmit analog. OVN kh√°c biŠĽát: t√°ch hŠļ≥n stage 23 cho rewrite + cluster-wide MAC_Binding qua SBDB cho ph√©p mŠĽći chassis share c√Ļng cache thay v√¨ hŠĽćc ri√™ng tŠĽęng host.

---

## ¬ß13.19.42 LR_IN_ARP_REQUEST ‚ÄĒ emit ARP/ND request khi MAC_Binding miss sau resolve

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LR_IN_ARP_REQUEST` l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 19** cŠĽßa LR ingress, OF table 27 tr√™n br-int (theo 13.16 d√≤ng 235). Stage l√† **ńĎiŠĽÉm cuŠĽĎi ingress LR**: nŠļŅu sau `LR_IN_ARP_RESOLVE` (stage 15) packet vŠļęn kh√īng c√≥ `eth.dst` hŠĽ£p lŠĽá (vŠļęn `00:00:00:00:00:00` placeholder), stage n√†y gŠĽći controller action emit g√≥i ARP/ND request ra outport ńĎŠĽÉ hŠĽćc MAC tŠĽę next-hop, ńĎŠĽďng thŠĽĚi (th∆įŠĽĚng) drop packet hiŠĽán tŠļ°i. LoŠļ°i: **pipeline ingress ARP emitter peripheral**, sub-loŠļ°i "neighbor solicitation generator".

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage logic 19, OF table 27 ‚ÄĒ stage cuŠĽĎi c√Ļng trong LR ingress. ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LR_IN_GW_REDIRECT` (stage 18, table 26) v√† l√† final stage tr∆įŠĽõc packet chuyŠĽÉn sang egress pipeline (qua `next_pipeline` action). Scope: per-packet kh√īng c√≥ MAC binding sau ARP_RESOLVE.

**Vai tr√≤ + v√¨ sao sinh ra.** Khi LR cŠļßn forward packet ńĎŠļŅn next-hop ch∆įa biŠļŅt MAC, phŠļ£i emit ARP request (IPv4) hoŠļ∑c ND solicitation (IPv6) ńĎŠĽÉ hŠĽćc. OVN t√°ch emit n√†y v√†o stage cuŠĽĎi c√Ļng ingress v√¨: (a) emit cŠļßn outport ńĎ√£ ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh, (b) drop packet hiŠĽán tŠļ°i tr√°nh re-buffer nŠĽôi bŠĽô datapath, (c) khi reply vŠĽĀ, `LR_IN_LEARN_NEIGHBOR` (stage 2) sŠļĹ insert MAC_Binding cho lŠļßn sau.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** (a) Trigger ARP/ND learning tŠĽę data plane, (b) gom ńĎiŠĽÉm emit vŠĽĀ mŠĽôt stage ńĎŠĽÉ rate-limit dŠĽÖ (avoid ARP storm), (c) t√°ch khŠĽŹi RESOLVE giŠĽĮ semantics r√Ķ r√†ng: RESOLVE = apply MAC, REQUEST = learn MAC, (d) cho ph√©p static drop (kh√īng emit) qua policy.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** H√†m sinh flow: `build_lrouter_arp_request_flows` trong `northd/northd.c` (token `S_ROUTER_IN_ARP_REQUEST`). Function sinh: (a) priority 100 match `eth.dst == 00:00:00:00:00:00 && ip4` ‚Üí action `arp { eth.dst = ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff; arp.spa = reg1; arp.tpa = reg0; arp.op = 1; output; }; output;` (build ARP request tŠĽę template + output); (b) priority 100 match `eth.dst == 00:00:00:00:00:00 && ip6` ‚Üí action `nd_ns { ... }; output;`; (c) priority 0 catch-all `output;`. V√≠ dŠĽ•:

```
table=27 (lr_in_arp_request), priority=100,
  match=(eth.dst == 00:00:00:00:00:00 && ip4),
  action=(arp { eth.dst = ff:ff:ff:ff:ff:ff;
                arp.spa = reg1; arp.tpa = reg0;
                arp.op = 1; output; };)
table=27, priority=0, match=(1), action=(output;)
```

Action `arp { ... }` l√† OVN compound action: clone packet, build ARP frame trong scope nested, emit ra outport. Original packet sau ńĎ√≥ drop (kh√īng c√≥ `output` cho ip4 path).

**Quy tr√¨nh + c√°ch quan s√°t.** Khi VM trong tenant gŠĽ≠i packet ńĎŠļßu ti√™n ńĎŠļŅn next-hop ch∆įa biŠļŅt MAC: ovn-trace b√°o packet ńĎŠļŅn table 27, action arp{} emit. `tcpdump -i br-int -e arp` thŠļ•y ARP request. Sau ~1ms, ARP reply vŠĽĀ ‚Üí `LR_IN_LEARN_NEIGHBOR` insert MAC_Binding ‚Üí packet thŠĽ© 2 sŠļĹ ńĎi qua b√¨nh th∆įŠĽĚng. `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=27` xem n_packets emit count.

**Kh√°c biŠĽát phi√™n bŠļ£n.** OVN < 21.03: emit logic embed trong ARP_RESOLVE, kh√īng t√°ch stage. OVN 21.03 t√°ch stage REQUEST ri√™ng. OVN 22.03 ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh. OVN 23.06 th√™m rate-limit `arp { }` ŠĽü pinctrl tr√°nh storm khi nhiŠĽĀu packet c√Ļng ńĎŠĽ£i c√Ļng next-hop. OVN 24.03 th√™m option `ovn-northd:arp_request_drop_threshold` cho ph√©p drop packet sau N retry kh√īng learn ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c MAC.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** Action `arp { }` + `nd_ns { }` compound action (parser `lib/actions.c`), `LR_IN_ARP_RESOLVE` (sister stage 15), `LR_IN_LEARN_NEIGHBOR` (consumer khi reply vŠĽĀ), MAC_Binding SBDB, `xxreg0` next-hop IP, `xxreg1` source IP cŠĽßa LRP. Xem 13.18 (REGBIT catalog), 13.5 ¬ß13.5.1c.3 (MAC_Binding), 13.16 d√≤ng 235. Loose: external gateway BFD (link liveness) ‚ÄĒ nŠļŅu gateway down, ARP request fail m√£i.

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.** `northd/northd.c` h√†m `build_lrouter_arp_request_flows` xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ stage `S_ROUTER_IN_ARP_REQUEST` table 19 logical, table 27 OF. Compound action parser `lib/actions.c` `parse_ARP`, `parse_ND_NS`. Runtime: emit qua `controller/ofctrl.c` (no upcall, action xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ in-datapath qua flow clone).

**SŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ + lŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p.** Symptom: cluster restart to√†n bŠĽô ‚Üí ARP storm broadcast tr√™n external VLAN ‚Üí switch upstream rate-limit ‚Üí packet drop h√†ng loŠļ°t. Mitigation: pre-populate Static_MAC_Binding cho gateway, cŠļ•u h√¨nh `ovn-northd:arp_request_drop_threshold` ńĎŠĽÉ giŠĽõi hŠļ°n retry, monitor `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=27 | grep n_packets` thŠļ•y spike. Common pitfall: route ńĎŠļŅn next-hop nŠļĪm ngo√†i subnet LRP ‚Üí ARP request gŠĽ≠i v√†o void ‚Üí MAC kh√īng bao giŠĽĚ hŠĽćc ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c.

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Linux `arp_solicit` kernel trigger emit ARP analog. Cisco IOS emit ARP khi forwarding lookup miss MAC analog. OVN kh√°c biŠĽát: t√°ch hŠļ≥n stage 19 + emit qua compound action data-plane (kh√īng upcall), giŠļ£m overhead so vŠĽõi pinctrl-based learning; cluster-wide MAC_Binding qua SBDB gi√ļp 1 chassis hŠĽćc, mŠĽći chassis h∆įŠĽüng.

## ¬ß13.19.43 LR_OUT_UNDNAT ‚ÄĒ ńĎŠļ£o DNAT cho reply packet rŠĽĚi router

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LR_OUT_UNDNAT` l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 1** cŠĽßa LR egress, OF table 41 tr√™n br-int (theo 13.16 d√≤ng 251). Stage l√† **ńĎŠĽĎi xŠĽ©ng vŠĽõi `LR_IN_DNAT`**: khi packet ingress ńĎ√£ bŠĽč DNAT (rewrite `ip.dst` tŠĽę floating IP sang internal IP), reply packet tr√™n chiŠĽĀu ng∆įŠĽ£c cŠļßn ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c un-DNAT ńĎŠĽÉ kh√īi phŠĽ•c `ip.src` vŠĽĀ floating IP gŠĽĎc tr∆įŠĽõc khi rŠĽĚi LR. Stage gŠĽći `ct(table=Y, zone=DNAT_zone, nat)` ńĎŠĽÉ conntrack tŠĽĪ nhŠļ≠n diŠĽán reply packet (qua 5-tuple match) v√† reverse NAT mapping. LoŠļ°i: **pipeline egress NAT reverser peripheral**, sub-loŠļ°i "DNAT reverse stage".

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage logic 1, OF table 41 ‚ÄĒ ńĎŠļßu egress LR pipeline. ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LR_OUT_CHECK_DNAT_LOCAL` (stage 0, table 40) v√† tr∆įŠĽõc `LR_OUT_POST_UNDNAT` (stage 2, table 42). Scope: per-packet egress LR c√≥ √≠t nhŠļ•t mŠĽôt NAT entry kiŠĽÉu DNAT (hoŠļ∑c dnat_and_snat). C√Ļng hŠĽć NAT family: `LR_IN_UNSNAT` (ńĎŠĽĎi xŠĽ©ng cho SNAT reverse) + `LR_OUT_SNAT` (forward SNAT) + `LR_IN_DNAT` (forward DNAT).

**Vai tr√≤ + v√¨ sao sinh ra.** Floating IP / port forwarding pattern y√™u cŠļßu connection tracking ńĎŠĽÉ reply tŠĽĪ ńĎŠĽông un-NAT. NŠļŅu ńĎŠĽÉ client outside thŠļ•y reply vŠĽõi internal IP (10.x), client sŠļĹ drop v√¨ 5-tuple kh√īng match connection ban ńĎŠļßu. Stage UNDNAT ńĎŠļ£m bŠļ£o invariant: tŠĽę ngo√†i thŠļ•y connection chŠĽČ qua floating IP, kh√īng leak internal topology.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** (a) Reverse DNAT mapping qua conntrack zone, (b) t√°ch reverse khŠĽŹi forward (DNAT ingress, UNDNAT egress) cho semantics r√Ķ r√†ng, (c) cho ph√©p DNAT zone ri√™ng biŠĽát vŠĽõi SNAT zone ńĎŠĽÉ hairpin scenarios kh√īng conflict, (d) ńĎŠļ£m bŠļ£o reply packet trong c√Ļng connection ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c un-NAT idempotent.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** H√†m sinh flow: `build_lrouter_out_undnat_flow` (per LB) + `build_lrouter_out_undnat_flow_normal_vip` trong `northd/northd.c` branch-22.03 (token `S_ROUTER_OUT_UNDNAT`). Function sinh flow priority 100 cho mŠĽói NAT entry kiŠĽÉu `dnat`/`dnat_and_snat`:

```
table=41 (lr_out_undnat), priority=100,
  match=(ip4 && ip4.src == 10.0.0.5 && outport == "lrp-uplink"
         && is_chassis_resident("cr-lrp-uplink")),
  action=(ct_dnat;)
table=41, priority=0, match=(1), action=(next;)
```

Action `ct_dnat` (kh√īng tham sŠĽĎ) tr√™n egress = "reverse DNAT cho packet trong conntrack zone hiŠĽán tŠļ°i". Conntrack tra entry vŠĽõi original tuple (10.0.0.5, ...) ‚Üí reverse mapping vŠĽĀ (192.0.2.10, ...) ‚Üí rewrite `ip.src`. Predicate `is_chassis_resident()` ńĎŠļ£m bŠļ£o chŠĽČ gateway chassis (cr port owner) thŠĽĪc thi UNDNAT centralized.

**Quy tr√¨nh + c√°ch quan s√°t.** Setup: `ovn-nbctl -- --id=@nat create NAT type=dnat_and_snat external_ip=192.0.2.10 logical_ip=10.0.0.5 -- add Logical_Router lr-main nat @nat`. VM 10.0.0.5 nhŠļ≠n packet inbound (DNAT ingress) ‚Üí reply. Trace: `ovn-trace lr-main 'inport=="lrp-vm" && ip4.src==10.0.0.5 && ip4.dst==<client>'` xem stage 41 emit `ct_dnat`. `conntrack -L -z <dnat_zone>` thŠļ•y entry. `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=41` xem n_packets.

**Kh√°c biŠĽát phi√™n bŠļ£n.** OVN 2.6 introduce DNAT/UNDNAT cŠļ∑p. OVN 20.06 t√°ch POST_UNDNAT (stage 2) ra ńĎŠĽÉ ch√®n policy giŠĽĮa undnat v√† snat. OVN 21.06 th√™m hairpin support qua `LR_OUT_CHECK_DNAT_LOCAL` (stage 0) skip undnat khi dest local. OVN 22.03 baseline ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh. OVN 23.06 tŠĽĎi ∆įu predicate `is_chassis_resident` cho distributed gateway. OVN 24.03 th√™m support `stateless` NAT bypass UNDNAT.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** `NAT` table NBDB (column `type=dnat`/`dnat_and_snat`, `external_ip`, `logical_ip`), `LR_IN_DNAT` (forward path t∆į∆°ng ŠĽ©ng, stage 6), `LR_OUT_POST_UNDNAT` (downstream stage 2), `LR_OUT_CHECK_DNAT_LOCAL` (upstream stage 0 skip cho hairpin), conntrack DNAT zone (column `Logical_Router.options:dnat_force_snat_ip` ńĎŠĽÉ force SNAT sau UNDNAT), action `ct_dnat`, predicate `is_chassis_resident`, kernel `nf_nat_module`. Xem 13.3 ¬ßNAT (NAT deep dive), 13.5 ¬ßport_binding chassisredirect, 13.16 d√≤ng 251.

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.** `northd/northd.c` h√†m `build_lrouter_out_undnat_flow` + `build_lrouter_out_undnat_flow_normal_vip` xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ stage `S_ROUTER_OUT_UNDNAT` table 1 logical, table 41 OF. Action `ct_dnat` parser `lib/actions.c` `parse_CT_DNAT_IN_V2`. Runtime: kernel `nf_nat_module` qua `ct()` hook OVS conntrack action.

**SŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ + lŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p.** Q1/2025 OpenStack-on-OVN: floating IP reply traffic drop random sau gateway failover. Cause: conntrack DNAT zone chŠĽČ tŠĽďn tŠļ°i tr√™n active gateway; sau failover, new gateway ch∆įa c√≥ entry ‚Üí reply kh√īng un-DNAT ‚Üí client thŠļ•y internal IP ‚Üí drop. Mitigation: enable `external_ids:always_learn_from_arp_request=true` ńĎŠļ©y NAT v√†o SBDB-replicated flow thay v√¨ chŠĽČ kernel conntrack; tńÉng `ovn-controller --conntrack-zone-replication` (nŠļŅu c√≥). Common pitfall: predicate `is_chassis_resident` mismatch khi cr port migrate ‚Üí packet kh√īng match bŠļ•t kŠĽ≥ flow priority 100 n√†o ‚Üí fallthrough m√† ch∆įa un-NAT.

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Linux iptables `-t nat -A POSTROUTING ... -j SNAT` + conntrack reverse mapping analog. Cisco IOS `ip nat outside source` analog. OVN kh√°c biŠĽát: explicit stage trong pipeline, declarative qua NAT row NBDB, conntrack zone t√°ch ri√™ng cho DNAT vs SNAT gi√ļp hairpin scenarios chŠļ°y kh√īng conflict; `is_chassis_resident()` predicate ńĎŠļ£m bŠļ£o centralized execution tr√™n gateway chassis duy nhŠļ•t.

## ¬ß13.19.44 LR_OUT_DELIVERY ‚ÄĒ b√†n giao packet ra LRP egress hoŠļ∑c patch port

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LR_OUT_DELIVERY` l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 6** cŠĽßa LR egress, OF table 46 tr√™n br-int (theo 13.16 d√≤ng 256) ‚ÄĒ **stage cuŠĽĎi c√Ļng** cŠĽßa to√†n pipeline LR. Stage c√≥ nhiŠĽám vŠĽ• duy nhŠļ•t: emit packet ra physical realization cŠĽßa `outport` ńĎ√£ ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c set bŠĽüi IP_ROUTING. NŠļŅu `outport` l√† LRP nŠĽĎi vŠĽõi LSP (peer = LSP), packet ńĎ∆įŠĽ£c resubmit v√†o ingress pipeline LSP cŠĽßa switch peer (qua action `output`); nŠļŅu `outport` l√† LRP nŠĽĎi LR kh√°c qua patch port, packet ńĎi qua patch peer; nŠļŅu l√† chassisredirect (cr) port, output qua tunnel Geneve ńĎŠļŅn gateway chassis. LoŠļ°i: **pipeline egress final delivery peripheral**, sub-loŠļ°i "physical output gate".

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage logic 6, OF table 46 ‚ÄĒ last stage egress LR. ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LR_OUT_EGR_LOOP` (stage 5, table 45). Sau stage n√†y packet rŠĽĚi LR pipeline ho√†n to√†n. Scope: every packet rŠĽĚi LR phŠļ£i ńĎi qua ńĎ√Ęy.

**Vai tr√≤ + v√¨ sao sinh ra.** T√°ch "delivery" ra stage ri√™ng v√¨: (a) IP_ROUTING chŠĽČ set logical outport (LRP name), kh√īng biŠļŅt physical realization; (b) chassisredirect cŠļßn encapsulation tunnel kh√°c vŠĽõi patch port direct; (c) emit kh√°c nhau giŠĽĮa "LR ‚Üí LSP next" (phŠļ£i resubmit ingress LSP) v√† "LR ‚Üí external network" (output qua LRP-bound port); (d) stage cuŠĽĎi cŇ©ng l√† ńĎiŠĽÉm logging + drop counter cho egress.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** (a) Routing decision (logical) t√°ch khŠĽŹi delivery (physical), (b) chassisredirect resolution (LRP_local hay output qua tunnel), (c) hŠĽó trŠĽ£ LRP peer = LSP (resubmit pipeline LSP) hoŠļ∑c patch port (emit qua peer's table 0), (d) gom ńĎiŠĽÉm logging/drop counter cho egress.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** H√†m sinh flow: `build_lrouter_out_delivery` trong `northd/northd.c` branch-22.03 (token `S_ROUTER_OUT_DELIVERY`). Function sinh flow priority 110 cho mŠĽói LRP cŠĽ• thŠĽÉ vŠĽõi match `outport == "lrp-name"` ‚Üí action `output;`. Predicate xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ chassisredirect ri√™ng:

```
table=46 (lr_out_delivery), priority=110,
  match=(outport == "lrp-vm" && !is_chassis_resident("lrp-vm")),
  action=(drop;)
table=46, priority=100,
  match=(outport == "lrp-vm"),
  action=(output;)
table=46, priority=0, match=(1), action=(drop;)
```

Action `output` ŠĽü ńĎ√Ęy emit packet qua port li√™n kŠļŅt LRP ‚ÄĒ controller resolve LRP ‚Üí patch port ‚Üí ingress pipeline LSP peer (hoŠļ∑c tunnel encap nŠļŅu LSP peer remote). Predicate `!is_chassis_resident()` drop packet kh√īng thuŠĽôc chassis hiŠĽán tŠļ°i ńĎŠĽÉ tr√°nh duplicate output tr√™n cluster.

**Quy tr√¨nh + c√°ch quan s√°t.** `ovn-sbctl lflow-list lr-main | grep lr_out_delivery` xem flow per LRP. `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=46` xem n_packets per outport. `ovn-trace` th∆įŠĽĚng kŠļŅt th√ļc vŠĽõi "output to lrp-name" b√°o packet ńĎŠļŅn stage 46 th√†nh c√īng. Khi stage drop (priority 0 catch-all), kiŠĽÉm tra `outport` c√≥ set ńĎ√ļng kh√īng (th∆įŠĽĚng do IP_ROUTING kh√īng match prefix).

**Kh√°c biŠĽát phi√™n bŠļ£n.** OVN 2.6 introduce stage DELIVERY ńĎ∆°n giŠļ£n (chŠĽČ output). OVN 20.06 th√™m `is_chassis_resident` predicate cho distributed gateway. OVN 21.06 th√™m support LRP c√≥ nhiŠĽĀu chassis backing (HA_Chassis_Group). OVN 22.03 baseline ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh. OVN 24.03 cŠļ£i thiŠĽán priority handling khi LRP c√≥ cŠļ£ gateway_chassis v√† HA_Chassis_Group config.

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** `Port_Binding.type` = `patch`/`l3gateway`/`chassisredirect` (downstream consumer phŠĽ• thuŠĽôc loŠļ°i), `Logical_Router_Port` NBDB (define LRP), `LR_IN_GW_REDIRECT` (upstream stage 18, decide chassisredirect path), `LR_IN_IP_ROUTING` (set outport), action `output`, predicate `is_chassis_resident`. Xem 13.5 ¬ßport_binding catalog (8 type), 13.16 d√≤ng 256, 13.5b cho cr port type.

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.** `northd/northd.c` h√†m `build_lrouter_out_delivery` xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ stage `S_ROUTER_OUT_DELIVERY` table 6 logical, table 46 OF. Action `output` parser `lib/actions.c`. Runtime: `controller/physical.c` resolve `outport` ‚Üí OF action (output qua patch peer hoŠļ∑c tunnel encap vŠĽõi Geneve TLV).

**SŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ + lŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p.** Symptom: traffic egress LR drop ŠĽü stage 46 priority 0. Cause th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p: (a) `outport` kh√īng set (route kh√īng match prefix), (b) `is_chassis_resident` mismatch sau LRP migrate (HA_Chassis_Group failover ch∆įa propagate ńĎŠļßy ńĎŠĽß), (c) LRP peer LSP ńĎ√£ bŠĽč x√≥a nh∆įng route entry stale. Diagnose: `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=46 priority=0 | grep n_packets` thŠļ•y spike ‚Üí packet ńĎŠļŅn nh∆įng kh√īng match. Mitigation: re-check NB.NAT + Logical_Router_Static_Route consistency, force ovn-controller resync.

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Linux kernel `dev_queue_xmit` final emit point analog (per-net-device). Cisco IOS `egress interface output` analog. OVN kh√°c biŠĽát: t√°ch hŠļ≥n delivery th√†nh stage logical, cho ph√©p predicate per-chassis (`is_chassis_resident`) ńĎŠļ£m bŠļ£o chŠĽČ mŠĽôt chassis emit cho distributed scenarios; hŠĽó trŠĽ£ multi-realization (patch, l3gateway, cr) qua c√Ļng action `output` nh∆įng controller resolve kh√°c.

---

## ¬ß13.19.45 LR_OUT_EGR_LOOP ‚ÄĒ ph√°t hiŠĽán v√† t√°i ti√™m packet qua chassisredirect

**Kh√°i niŠĽám.** `LR_OUT_EGR_LOOP` (ńĎ√īi khi gŠĽći tŠļĮt "egress loopback stage") l√† stage logic **sŠĽĎ 5** cŠĽßa LR egress, OF table 45 tr√™n br-int (theo 13.16 d√≤ng 255). Stage c√≥ hai nhiŠĽám vŠĽ• ch√©o: (a) ph√°t hiŠĽán packet bŠĽč routing loop quay vŠĽĀ ch√≠nh LR (rare nh∆įng xŠļ£y ra vŠĽõi policy routing sai cŠļ•u h√¨nh hoŠļ∑c dnat_and_snat hairpin) v√† (b) t√°i ti√™m packet trŠĽü lŠļ°i ingress pipeline khi chassisredirect y√™u cŠļßu (gateway chassis nhŠļ≠n packet tŠĽę tunnel cŠļßn chŠļ°y ingress pipeline local thay v√¨ re-tunnel). Stage sŠĽ≠ dŠĽ•ng `REGBIT_EGRESS_LOOPBACK=reg9[0]` (xem 13.18 + 13.17) l√†m cŠĽĚ ńĎ√°nh dŠļ•u packet ńĎang trong v√≤ng loopback. LoŠļ°i: **pipeline egress loopback gate peripheral**, sub-loŠļ°i "hairpin + chassisredirect re-injection".

**VŠĽč tr√≠ trong kiŠļŅn tr√ļc.** Stage logic 5, OF table 45. ńźŠĽ©ng sau `LR_OUT_POST_SNAT` (stage 4, table 44) v√† tr∆įŠĽõc `LR_OUT_DELIVERY` (stage 6, table 46). Scope: per-packet, ńĎŠļ∑c biŠĽát quan trŠĽćng cho LR c√≥ distributed gateway (chassisredirect port) hoŠļ∑c dnat_and_snat hairpin scenarios.

**Vai tr√≤ + v√¨ sao sinh ra.** Hai use case ch√≠nh:

1. **Loop prevention.** Khi packet bŠĽč routing loop (vd. policy routing redirect packet vŠĽĀ ch√≠nh LR), bit `REGBIT_EGRESS_LOOPBACK` ńĎ√£ set tŠĽę v√≤ng tr∆įŠĽõc ‚Üí stage drop ńĎŠĽÉ chŠļ∑n v√≤ng v√ī hŠļ°n.
2. **Chassisredirect re-injection.** Khi gateway chassis nhŠļ≠n packet tŠĽę tunnel (packet ńĎ√£ ńĎi qua egress pipeline ŠĽü source chassis), cŠļßn re-inject v√†o ingress pipeline local ńĎŠĽÉ chŠļ°y SNAT/DNAT centralized; stage n√†y set `REGBIT_EGRESS_LOOPBACK=1` rŠĽďi resubmit vŠĽĀ ingress LR table 8.

**VŠļ•n ńĎŠĽĀ giŠļ£i quyŠļŅt.** (a) ChŠļ∑n routing loop infinite (an to√†n cŠļ•p datapath), (b) cho ph√©p gateway chassis chŠļ°y NAT centralized m√† kh√īng cŠļßn tunnel lŠļßn thŠĽ© 2, (c) t√°ch logic re-inject khŠĽŹi GW_REDIRECT (stage 18 ingress) ńĎŠĽÉ semantics ph√Ęn chia r√Ķ, (d) gom cŠĽĚ loopback vŠĽĀ mŠĽôt bit `reg9[0]` cho debug dŠĽÖ qua ovn-trace.

**C∆° chŠļŅ hoŠļ°t ńĎŠĽông.** H√†m sinh flow: `build_lrouter_egress_loopback_flow` (hoŠļ∑c `build_egress_loopback_flow` t∆į∆°ng ńĎ∆į∆°ng) trong `northd/northd.c` branch-22.03 (token `S_ROUTER_OUT_EGR_LOOP`). Function sinh: (a) priority 1000 match `reg9[0] == 1` ‚Üí `next;` (ńĎ√£ loopback rŠĽďi, cho qua, tr√°nh loop infinite); (b) priority 100 match cho hairpin scenario ‚Üí set `reg9[0] = 1; next(pipeline=ingress, table=0);`; (c) priority 0 catch-all `next;`. V√≠ dŠĽ• minh hoŠļ°:

```
table=45 (lr_out_egr_loop), priority=1000,
  match=(reg9[0] == 1),
  action=(next;)
table=45, priority=300,
  match=(ip4.dst == 192.0.2.10 && outport == "lrp-uplink"),
  action=(reg9[0] = 1;
          eth.dst <-> eth.src;
          next(pipeline=ingress, table=8);)
table=45, priority=0, match=(1), action=(next;)
```

H√†m `build_lrouter_egress_loopback_flow` (verified in `northd/northd.c` branch-22.03) ch√®n flow re-inject cho mŠĽói NAT row c√≥ `external_ip` t∆į∆°ng ŠĽ©ng hairpin VIP. Action `next(pipeline=ingress, table=N)` l√† OVN extension cho ph√©p cross-pipeline dispatch trong c√Ļng datapath.

**Quy tr√¨nh + c√°ch quan s√°t.** Hairpin scenario test: VM A gŠĽći floating IP cŠĽßa VM B (c√Ļng tenant LR). Packet ńĎi qua LR egress ńĎŠļŅn IP B ‚Üí stage 45 detect hairpin ‚Üí reg9[0]=1 ‚Üí re-inject ingress ‚Üí DNAT lookup ‚Üí forward ńĎŠļŅn B. Trace: `ovn-trace lr-main 'inport=="lrp-A" && ip4.dst==<B-FIP>'` thŠļ•y hai v√≤ng pipeline, bit reg9[0] flip giŠĽĮa. `ovs-ofctl dump-flows br-int table=45` xem n_packets cho tŠĽęng priority class.

**Kh√°c biŠĽát phi√™n bŠļ£n.** OVN 2.7 introduce REGBIT_EGRESS_LOOPBACK + stage. OVN 20.06 mŠĽü rŠĽông cho dnat_and_snat hairpin. OVN 21.06 th√™m support hairpin LB (separate stage ŠĽü LS, kh√īng Šļ£nh h∆įŠĽüng LR). OVN 22.03 baseline ŠĽēn ńĎŠĽčnh. OVN 24.03 cŠļ£i thiŠĽán priority ńĎŠĽÉ tr√°nh loop khi nested NAT (hairpin v√†o LR c√≥ DNAT nŠĽôi).

**Li√™n quan mŠļ≠t thiŠļŅt.** `REGBIT_EGRESS_LOOPBACK=reg9[0]` (definition `northd/northd.c`, sister bit family vŠĽõi REGBIT_PKT_LARGER, REGBIT_LOOKUP_NEIGHBOR_*), `LR_IN_GW_REDIRECT` (stage 18, ńĎŠĽĎi ŠĽ©ng cho path ńĎi xu√īi), `LR_OUT_DELIVERY` (downstream consumer khi kh√īng loopback), action `next(pipeline=ingress)` cross-dispatch, NAT table NBDB column `type=dnat_and_snat` (trigger hairpin). Xem 13.18 ¬ßREGBIT catalog d√≤ng REGBIT_EGRESS_LOOPBACK, 13.17 ¬ßlogical-fields.h, 13.16 d√≤ng 255, 19.0 ¬ßmulti-chassis hairpin.

**Source code tham chiŠļŅu.** `northd/northd.c` h√†m xŠĽ≠ l√Ĺ stage `S_ROUTER_OUT_EGR_LOOP` table 5 logical, table 45 OF (verified token branch-22.03 PIPELINE_STAGES enum). REGBIT ńĎŠĽčnh nghń©a `include/ovn/logical-fields.h` macro `REGBIT_EGRESS_LOOPBACK "reg9[0]"`. Action `next(pipeline=...)` parser `lib/actions.c` `parse_NEXT`. Cross-dispatch resolution `controller/lflow.c` apply `OFTABLE_LOG_INGRESS_PIPELINE` resubmit.

**SŠĽĪ cŠĽĎ thŠĽĪc tŠļŅ + lŠĽói th∆įŠĽĚng gŠļ∑p.** Q4/2024 cluster c√≥ 30 tenant LR vŠĽõi floating IP hairpin: traffic VM-to-VM c√Ļng tenant qua FIP ńĎ√īi khi loop hai v√≤ng pipeline g√Ęy latency tńÉng ~200¬Ķs. Diagnose: ovn-trace b√°o reg9[0] flip 1‚Üí0 sai do priority class conflict sau OVN upgrade 22.03 ‚Üí 23.06. Mitigation: rebuild lflow qua `ovn-nbctl --wait=hv sync`, verify priority 1000 catch loopback exit. Common pitfall: policy routing tŠļ°o loop v√ī t√¨nh ‚Üí packet ńĎi qua stage 45 nhiŠĽĀu lŠļßn vŠĽõi reg9[0]=1 ‚Üí priority 1000 cho qua ‚Üí vŠļęn loop v√¨ stage tiŠļŅp ingress redirect lŠļ°i ‚Üí cuŠĽĎi c√Ļng TTL=0 drop. Fix: simplify policy routing, d√Ļng `ovn-trace` xem mŠĽói v√≤ng.

**So s√°nh vŠĽõi hŠĽá kh√°c.** Linux iptables `-m conntrack --ctstate DNAT -j MARK ... ; -j MASQUERADE` cho hairpin analog (per-host). VMware NSX-T hairpin vNIC analog (per-edge gateway). OVN kh√°c biŠĽát: REGBIT bit dedicated trong logical pipeline cho ph√©p cross-pipeline dispatch declarative; gateway chassis re-inject m√† kh√īng cŠļßn tunnel encap th√™m; semantics r√Ķ r√†ng giŠĽĮa "loop prevention" v√† "intentional re-injection" qua priority class.

## Stage thŠĽ© cŠļ•p + ngoŠļ°i bi√™n (xem 13.16 cho table ID ńĎŠļßy ńĎŠĽß)


### LS_IN secondary (M16, ~10 stage)

LS_IN_LB_AFF_*, LS_IN_PRE_HAIRPIN, LS_IN_NAT_HAIRPIN, LS_IN_HAIRPIN, LS_IN_ARP_ND_RSP, LS_IN_DHCP_RESPONSE.

### LS_IN peripheral (P21, ~12 stage)

LS_IN_PORT_SEC_IP, LS_IN_PORT_SEC_ND, LS_IN_LOOKUP_FDB, LS_IN_PUT_FDB, LS_IN_PRE_STATEFUL, LS_IN_LB_AFF_LEARN, etc.

### LS_OUT (M16 + P21, 11 stage)

LS_OUT_PRE_LB, LS_OUT_ACL, LS_OUT_PORT_SEC_L2, etc.

### LR_IN secondary (M17 + P22, 9 stage)

LR_IN_DEFRAG, LR_IN_UNSNAT, LR_IN_LARGER_PKTS, LR_IN_LOOKUP_NEIGHBOR, LEARN_NEIGHBOR, IP_ROUTING, IP_ROUTING_ECMP, POLICY, POLICY_ECMP. (Stage `LR_IN_ARP_RESOLVE` ńĎ√£ c√≥ treatment ńĎŠļßy ńĎŠĽß ŠĽü ¬ß13.19.41; `LR_IN_ARP_REQUEST` ŠĽü ¬ß13.19.42.)

### LR_OUT (M17 + P22, 6 stage)

LR_OUT_POST_UNDNAT, LR_OUT_SNAT, etc. (Stage `LR_OUT_UNDNAT` ńĎ√£ c√≥ treatment ńĎŠļßy ńĎŠĽß ŠĽü ¬ß13.19.43; `LR_OUT_DELIVERY` ŠĽü ¬ß13.19.44; `LR_OUT_EGR_LOOP` (egress loopback) ŠĽü ¬ß13.19.45.)
